```
//! Configuration types for agents and the swarm runtime.

use std::time::Duration;

use figment::{
    Figment,
    providers::{Env, Format, Serialized, Toml},
};
use serde::Deserialize;

/// Controls how the supervisor restarts a failed agent.
///
/// The supervisor tracks restart timestamps within a rolling [`window`](Self::window).
/// If the agent is restarted more than [`max_restarts`](Self::max_restarts) times
/// within that window, the supervisor gives up. Each restart waits for an
/// exponentially increasing backoff, capped at [`backoff_max`](Self::backoff_max).
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct RestartPolicy {
    /// Maximum number of restarts allowed within `window` before giving up.
    pub max_restarts: u32,
    /// Rolling time window for counting restarts.
    pub window: Duration,
    /// Initial backoff duration after the first restart.
    pub backoff_base: Duration,
    /// Maximum backoff duration (caps exponential growth).
    pub backoff_max: Duration,
}

impl Default for RestartPolicy {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            max_restarts: 5,
            window: Duration::from_secs(60),
            backoff_base: Duration::from_secs(1),
            backoff_max: Duration::from_secs(30),
        }
    }
}

/// Per-agent configuration.
///
/// Created with [`AgentConfig::new`] and customized via builder methods.
///
/// # Example
///
/// ```
/// use mra::config::{AgentConfig, RestartPolicy};
///
/// let config = AgentConfig::new("researcher")
///     .with_mailbox_size(64)
///     .with_restart_policy(RestartPolicy {
///         max_restarts: 10,
///         ..Default::default()
///     });
/// ```
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct AgentConfig {
    /// Human-readable name for logging and tracing.
    pub name: String,
    /// Bounded channel capacity for this agent's inbox.
    pub mailbox_size: usize,
    /// Supervisor restart behavior for this agent.
    pub restart_policy: RestartPolicy,
}

impl AgentConfig {
    /// Creates a new agent config with the given name and sensible defaults.
    pub fn new(name: impl Into<String>) -> Self {
        Self {
            name: name.into(),
            mailbox_size: 8,
            restart_policy: RestartPolicy::default(),
        }
    }

    /// Sets the bounded channel capacity for this agent's inbox.
    pub fn with_mailbox_size(mut self, size: usize) -> Self {
        self.mailbox_size = size;
        self
    }

    /// Sets the supervisor restart policy for this agent.
    pub fn with_restart_policy(mut self, policy: RestartPolicy) -> Self {
        self.restart_policy = policy;
        self
    }
}

/// Global runtime configuration for the swarm.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct RuntimeConfig {
    /// Maximum number of agents the runtime will accept.
    pub max_agents: usize,
    /// Hard timeout for graceful shutdown before aborting remaining tasks.
    pub shutdown_timeout: Duration,
}

impl Default for RuntimeConfig {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            max_agents: 100,
            shutdown_timeout: Duration::from_secs(30),
        }
    }
}

/// LLM provider configuration.
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Deserialize)]
pub struct LlmConfig {
    pub api_key: String,
    pub model: String,
    pub base_url: String,
}

/// File-friendly runtime configuration with seconds instead of `Duration`.
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Deserialize, serde::Serialize)]
pub struct RuntimeConfigFile {
    pub max_agents: usize,
    pub shutdown_timeout_secs: u64,
}

/// Top-level configuration loaded from `mra.toml` + env vars.
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Deserialize)]
pub struct MraConfig {
    pub llm: LlmConfig,
    pub runtime: RuntimeConfigFile,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Serialize, Deserialize)]
struct MraConfigDefaults {
    llm: LlmConfigDefaults,
    runtime: RuntimeConfigFile,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Serialize, Deserialize)]
struct LlmConfigDefaults {
    api_key: String,
    model: String,
    base_url: String,
}

impl Default for MraConfigDefaults {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            llm: LlmConfigDefaults {
                api_key: String::new(),
                model: "openai/gpt-4o-mini".into(),
                base_url: "https://openrouter.ai/api/v1".into(),
            },
            runtime: RuntimeConfigFile {
                max_agents: 100,
                shutdown_timeout_secs: 30,
            },
        }
    }
}

impl MraConfig {
    /// Loads config: defaults → `mra.toml` → `MRA_` env vars.
    #[allow(clippy::result_large_err)]
    pub fn load() -> Result<Self, figment::Error> {
        Figment::new()
            .merge(Serialized::defaults(MraConfigDefaults::default()))
            .merge(Toml::file("mra.toml"))
            .merge(Env::prefixed("MRA_").split("__"))
            .extract()
    }

    /// Returns a config with only hardcoded defaults.
    pub fn defaults() -> Self {
        let d = MraConfigDefaults::default();
        Self {
            llm: LlmConfig {
                api_key: d.llm.api_key,
                model: d.llm.model,
                base_url: d.llm.base_url,
            },
            runtime: d.runtime,
        }
    }

    /// Converts to the runtime's [`RuntimeConfig`].
    pub fn runtime_config(&self) -> RuntimeConfig {
        RuntimeConfig {
            max_agents: self.runtime.max_agents,
            shutdown_timeout: Duration::from_secs(self.runtime.shutdown_timeout_secs),
        }
    }
}
```

//! Supervisor system — Erlang/OTP-style agent lifecycle management.

pub(crate) mod child;
mod config;
mod event;
mod handle;
pub(crate) mod runner;
pub(crate) mod tracker;

pub use child::{ChildContext, ChildFactory, ChildSpec, SpawnedChild};
pub use config::{ChildRestart, RestartIntensity, ShutdownPolicy, Strategy, SupervisorConfig};
pub use event::SupervisorEvent;
pub use handle::SupervisorHandle;

/// Why a child agent exited.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub enum ChildExit {
    /// Clean return from the agent's run loop (channel closed, no senders left).
    Normal,
    /// Explicit shutdown via cancellation token or shutdown message.
    Shutdown,
    /// The agent's behavior handler returned an error.
    Failed(String),
}

impl ChildExit {
    /// Returns `true` if this exit should trigger a restart
    /// (for `Transient` or `Permanent` restart policies).
    pub fn is_failure(&self) -> bool {
        matches!(self, Self::Failed(_))
    }
}
```

```
use std::time::Duration;

use super::ChildExit;

/// Lifecycle events emitted by the supervisor via a `broadcast` channel.
///
/// Subscribe with [`SupervisorHandle::subscribe`](super::SupervisorHandle::subscribe)
/// to observe starts, stops, restarts, and hang detections.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub enum SupervisorEvent {
    /// The supervisor's event loop has started.
    SupervisorStarted,
    /// The supervisor is draining children before shutting down.
    SupervisorStopping,
    /// A child was spawned (or respawned) successfully.
    ChildStarted { name: String, generation: u64 },
    /// A child's run future completed.
    ChildExited {
        name: String,
        generation: u64,
        exit: ChildExit,
    },
    /// A child was restarted after a failure, with the backoff `delay` applied.
    ChildRestarted {
        name: String,
        old_gen: u64,
        new_gen: u64,
        delay: Duration,
    },
    /// A child has been busy without reporting progress longer than its timeout.
    HangDetected {
        name: String,
        generation: u64,
        elapsed: Duration,
    },
    /// A single child hit its per-child restart limit and will not be restarted again.
    ChildRestartLimitExceeded { name: String, restarts: u64 },
    /// Supervisor-wide restart intensity exceeded — the supervisor shuts down.
    RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts: u64 },
    /// A token budget was exceeded (reserved for future event-emitter wiring).
    BudgetExceeded { name: String, used: u64, limit: u64 },
}
```

```
//! Supervisor system — Erlang/OTP-style agent lifecycle management.

pub(crate) mod child;
mod config;
mod event;
mod handle;
pub(crate) mod runner;
pub(crate) mod tracker;

pub use child::{ChildContext, ChildFactory, ChildSpec, SpawnedChild};
pub use config::{ChildRestart, RestartIntensity, ShutdownPolicy, Strategy, SupervisorConfig};
pub use event::SupervisorEvent;
pub use handle::SupervisorHandle;

/// Why a child agent exited.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub enum ChildExit {
    /// Clean return from the agent's run loop (channel closed, no senders left).
    Normal,
    /// Explicit shutdown via cancellation token or shutdown message.
    Shutdown,
    /// The agent's behavior handler returned an error.
    Failed(String),
}

impl ChildExit {
    /// Returns `true` if this exit should trigger a restart
    /// (for `Transient` or `Permanent` restart policies).
    pub fn is_failure(&self) -> bool {
        matches!(self, Self::Failed(_))
    }
}

### Tool Call [completed]: Read /Users/yuan/Developer/mra/src/supervisor/runner.rs

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-03-28 23:40:03

```
use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::sync::Arc;
use std::time::Duration;

use tokio::sync::{broadcast, mpsc, watch};
use tokio::task::JoinSet;
use tokio_util::sync::CancellationToken;

use crate::agent::AgentHandle;
use crate::agent::ProgressState;
use crate::agent::mailbox::MailboxSlot;
use crate::budget::BudgetTracker;
use crate::error::SupervisorError;
use crate::ids::AgentId;
use crate::tool::ToolRegistry;

use super::ChildExit;
use super::child::{ChildContext, ChildSpec};
use super::config::{ChildRestart, Strategy, SupervisorConfig};
use super::event::SupervisorEvent;
use super::handle::SupervisorCommand;
use super::tracker::{IntensityTracker, RestartTracker};

struct ChildState {
    spec: ChildSpec,
    id: AgentId,
    generation: u64,
    progress: Option<watch::Receiver<ProgressState>>,
    child_cancel: Option<CancellationToken>,
    mailbox: Arc<MailboxSlot>,
    logical_cancel: CancellationToken,
    tracker: RestartTracker,
    alive: bool,
    hung: bool,
}

pub(crate) struct SupervisorRunner {
    config: SupervisorConfig,
    children: HashMap<String, ChildState>,
    child_order: Vec<String>,
    task_map: HashMap<tokio::task::Id, String>,
    join_set: JoinSet<ChildExit>,
    command_rx: mpsc::Receiver<SupervisorCommand>,
    event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>,
    cancel: CancellationToken,
    intensity: IntensityTracker,
    budget: Option<Arc<BudgetTracker>>,
}

impl SupervisorRunner {
    pub(crate) fn new(
        config: SupervisorConfig,
        command_rx: mpsc::Receiver<SupervisorCommand>,
        event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>,
        budget: Option<Arc<BudgetTracker>>,
    ) -> Self {
        let intensity = IntensityTracker::new(config.intensity.clone());
        Self {
            config,
            children: HashMap::new(),
            child_order: Vec::new(),
            task_map: HashMap::new(),
            join_set: JoinSet::new(),
            command_rx,
            event_tx,
            cancel: CancellationToken::new(),
            intensity,
            budget,
        }
    }

    pub(crate) async fn run(mut self) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        let mut hang_tick = tokio::time::interval(self.config.hang_check_interval);
        hang_tick.set_missed_tick_behavior(tokio::time::MissedTickBehavior::Skip);

        self.emit(SupervisorEvent::SupervisorStarted);

        loop {
            tokio::select! {
                _ = self.cancel.cancelled() => {
                    self.drain_all().await;
                    break Ok(());
                }

                Some(result) = self.join_set.join_next_with_id() => {
                    self.handle_child_exit(result).await?;
                }

                cmd = self.command_rx.recv() => match cmd {
                    None => {
                        self.drain_all().await;
                        break Ok(());
                    }
                    Some(cmd) => self.handle_command(cmd).await?,
                },

                _ = hang_tick.tick() => {
                    self.check_hangs().await;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    fn emit(&self, event: SupervisorEvent) {
        let _ = self.event_tx.send(event);
    }

    async fn handle_command(&mut self, cmd: SupervisorCommand) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        match cmd {
            SupervisorCommand::StartChild { spec, reply } => {
                let result = self.do_start_child(spec).await;
                let _ = reply.send(result);
            }
            SupervisorCommand::StopChild { name, reply } => {
                let result = self.do_stop_child(&name).await;
                let _ = reply.send(result);
            }
            SupervisorCommand::GetChild { name, reply } => {
                let handle = self.children.get(&name).map(|child| {
                    AgentHandle::new(
                        child.id,
                        child.mailbox.clone(),
                        child.logical_cancel.clone(),
                    )
                });
                let _ = reply.send(handle);
            }
            SupervisorCommand::Shutdown => {
                self.drain_all().await;
                self.cancel.cancel();
            }
        }
        Ok(())
    }

    async fn do_start_child(&mut self, spec: ChildSpec) -> Result<AgentHandle, SupervisorError> {
        let name = spec.name.clone();
        let id = AgentId::new();
        let logical_cancel = CancellationToken::new();
        let child_cancel = logical_cancel.child_token();

        // Create stable mailbox with dummy sender
        let (dummy_tx, _) = mpsc::channel(1);
        let mailbox = Arc::new(MailboxSlot::new(dummy_tx));

        // Build peers map from existing alive children
        let peers: HashMap<String, AgentHandle> = self
            .children
            .iter()
            .filter(|(_, c)| c.alive)
            .map(|(n, c)| {
                (
                    n.clone(),
                    AgentHandle::new(c.id, c.mailbox.clone(), c.logical_cancel.clone()),
                )
            })
            .collect();

        // Register agent budget slot if budget tracking is active
        if let Some(ref budget) = self.budget {
            budget.register_agent(&name, spec.token_budget);
        }

        // Call factory
        let ctx = ChildContext {
            id,
            generation: 0,
            cancel: child_cancel.clone(),
            peers,
            llm: None,
            budget: self.budget.clone(),
            tools: ToolRegistry::new(),
        };
        let spawned = (spec.factory)(ctx)
            .await
            .map_err(|e| SupervisorError::SpawnFailed(e.to_string()))?;

        // Swap real sender into stable mailbox
        mailbox.swap(spawned.sender);

        // Build the stable handle
        let handle = AgentHandle::new(id, mailbox.clone(), logical_cancel.clone());

        // Spawn future in JoinSet
        let abort = self.join_set.spawn(spawned.future);
        let task_id = abort.id();
        self.task_map.insert(task_id, name.clone());

        let tracker = RestartTracker::new(&spec.config.restart_policy);

        let state = ChildState {
            spec,
            id,
            generation: 0,
            progress: Some(spawned.progress),
            child_cancel: Some(child_cancel),
            mailbox,
            logical_cancel,
            tracker,
            alive: true,
            hung: false,
        };

        self.children.insert(name.clone(), state);
        self.child_order.push(name.clone());

        self.emit(SupervisorEvent::ChildStarted {
            name,
            generation: 0,
        });

        Ok(handle)
    }

    async fn do_stop_child(&mut self, name: &str) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        let child = self
            .children
            .get_mut(name)
            .ok_or_else(|| SupervisorError::ChildNotFound(name.into()))?;

        if let Some(cancel) = child.child_cancel.take() {
            cancel.cancel();
        }
        child.alive = false;
        Ok(())
    }

    async fn handle_child_exit(
        &mut self,
        result: Result<(tokio::task::Id, ChildExit), tokio::task::JoinError>,
    ) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        let (task_id, exit) = match result {
            Ok((id, exit)) => (id, exit),
            Err(e) => {
                let id = e.id();
                (id, ChildExit::Failed(format!("task panicked: {e}")))
            }
        };

        let Some(name) = self.task_map.remove(&task_id) else {
            return Ok(());
        };

        let (old_gen, should_restart) = {
            let Some(child) = self.children.get_mut(&name) else {
                return Ok(());
            };

            let old_gen = child.generation;
            child.alive = false;
            child.child_cancel = None;
            child.progress = None;

            // Hung children exit with Shutdown, which isn't a "failure" —
            // override so Transient restart policy still kicks in.
            let is_failure = if child.hung {
                child.hung = false;
                true
            } else {
                exit.is_failure()
            };
            let should_restart = child.spec.restart.should_restart(is_failure);
            (old_gen, should_restart)
        };

        let _ = self.event_tx.send(SupervisorEvent::ChildExited {
            name: name.clone(),
            generation: old_gen,
            exit,
        });

        if !should_restart || self.cancel.is_cancelled() {
            return Ok(());
        }

        match self.config.strategy {
            Strategy::OneForOne => {
                // Record in per-child tracker
                let now = tokio::time::Instant::now();
                let child = self.children.get_mut(&name).unwrap();
                child.tracker.record(now);

                if child.tracker.exceeded() {
                    let restarts = child.tracker.total_restarts;
                    let _ = self
                        .event_tx
                        .send(SupervisorEvent::ChildRestartLimitExceeded { name, restarts });
                    return Ok(());
                }

                // Record in per-supervisor intensity tracker
                self.intensity.record(now);
                if self.intensity.exceeded() {
                    let total_restarts = self.intensity.total_restarts;
                    let _ = self
                        .event_tx
                        .send(SupervisorEvent::RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts });
                    self.drain_all().await;
                    return Err(SupervisorError::RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts });
                }

                // Compute backoff delay and sleep
                let child = self.children.get(&name).unwrap();
                let delay = child.tracker.backoff_delay();
                tokio::time::sleep(delay).await;

                // Don't restart if cancelled during backoff sleep
                if self.cancel.is_cancelled() {
                    return Ok(());
                }

                // Build peers map from alive siblings
                let peers: HashMap<String, AgentHandle> = self
                    .children
                    .iter()
                    .filter(|(n, c)| c.alive && *n != &name)
                    .map(|(n, c)| {
                        (
                            n.clone(),
                            AgentHandle::new(c.id, c.mailbox.clone(), c.logical_cancel.clone()),
                        )
                    })
                    .collect();

                let child = self.children.get_mut(&name).unwrap();

                // Increment generation and create new per-generation cancel token
                let new_gen = old_gen + 1;
                let child_cancel = child.logical_cancel.child_token();

                let ctx = ChildContext {
                    id: child.id,
                    generation: new_gen,
                    cancel: child_cancel.clone(),
                    peers,
                    llm: None,
                    budget: self.budget.clone(),
                    tools: ToolRegistry::new(),
                };

                let spawned = match (child.spec.factory)(ctx).await {
                    Ok(s) => s,
                    Err(_) => {
                        // Factory failed — leave child dead
                        return Ok(());
                    }
                };

                // Hot-swap sender into stable mailbox
                child.mailbox.swap(spawned.sender);

                // Spawn new future in JoinSet
                let abort = self.join_set.spawn(spawned.future);
                let new_task_id = abort.id();
                self.task_map.insert(new_task_id, name.clone());

                // Update child state
                child.generation = new_gen;
                child.progress = Some(spawned.progress);
                child.child_cancel = Some(child_cancel);
                child.alive = true;

                let _ = self.event_tx.send(SupervisorEvent::ChildRestarted {
                    name,
                    old_gen,
                    new_gen,
                    delay,
                });
            }
            Strategy::OneForAll => {
                self.restart_all(&name).await?;
            }
        }

        Ok(())
    }

    async fn restart_all(&mut self, trigger_name: &str) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        // 1. Cancel all alive children (except the one that already exited)
        for (name, child) in &self.children {
            if name != trigger_name
                && let Some(ref cancel) = child.child_cancel
            {
                cancel.cancel();
            }
        }

        // 2. Wait for all to exit
        while self.join_set.join_next().await.is_some() {}
        self.task_map.clear();

        // 3. Record restart in per-supervisor intensity tracker
        let now = tokio::time::Instant::now();
        self.intensity.record(now);
        if self.intensity.exceeded() {
            let total = self.intensity.total_restarts;
            let _ = self
                .event_tx
                .send(SupervisorEvent::RestartIntensityExceeded {
                    total_restarts: total,
                });
            self.drain_all().await;
            return Err(SupervisorError::RestartIntensityExceeded {
                total_restarts: total,
            });
        }

        // 4. Respawn all non-Temporary children in insertion order
        let order = self.child_order.clone();
        for child_name in &order {
            // Skip Temporary children
            {
                let child = self.children.get_mut(child_name).unwrap();
                if matches!(child.spec.restart, ChildRestart::Temporary) {
                    child.alive = false;
                    continue;
                }
            }

            if self.cancel.is_cancelled() {
                return Ok(());
            }

            let (old_gen, new_gen, child_cancel, child_id) = {
                let child = self.children.get(child_name).unwrap();
                let old_gen = child.generation;
                let new_gen = old_gen + 1;
                let child_cancel = child.logical_cancel.child_token();
                (old_gen, new_gen, child_cancel, child.id)
            };

            // Build peers from already-respawned siblings
            let peers: HashMap<String, AgentHandle> = self
                .children
                .iter()
                .filter(|(n, c)| c.alive && *n != child_name)
                .map(|(n, c)| {
                    (
                        n.clone(),
                        AgentHandle::new(c.id, c.mailbox.clone(), c.logical_cancel.clone()),
                    )
                })
                .collect();

            let child = self.children.get_mut(child_name).unwrap();
            let ctx = ChildContext {
                id: child_id,
                generation: new_gen,
                cancel: child_cancel.clone(),
                peers,
                llm: None,
                budget: self.budget.clone(),
                tools: ToolRegistry::new(),
            };

            let spawned = match (child.spec.factory)(ctx).await {
                Ok(s) => s,
                Err(_) => {
                    child.alive = false;
                    continue;
                }
            };

            child.mailbox.swap(spawned.sender);
            let abort = self.join_set.spawn(spawned.future);
            self.task_map.insert(abort.id(), child_name.clone());

            child.generation = new_gen;
            child.progress = Some(spawned.progress);
            child.child_cancel = Some(child_cancel);
            child.alive = true;
            child.tracker.record(now);

            let _ = self.event_tx.send(SupervisorEvent::ChildRestarted {
                name: child_name.clone(),
                old_gen,
                new_gen,
                delay: Duration::from_millis(0),
            });
        }

        Ok(())
    }

    async fn drain_all(&mut self) {
        self.emit(SupervisorEvent::SupervisorStopping);
        for child in self.children.values() {
            if let Some(ref cancel) = child.child_cancel {
                cancel.cancel();
            }
        }
        while self.join_set.join_next().await.is_some() {}
    }

    async fn check_hangs(&mut self) {
        let mut hangs = Vec::new();

        for (name, child) in &self.children {
            if !child.alive {
                continue;
            }
            let Some(hang_timeout) = child.spec.hang_timeout else {
                continue;
            };
            let Some(ref progress_rx) = child.progress else {
                continue;
            };

            let progress = progress_rx.borrow();
            if progress.busy && progress.last_progress.elapsed() > hang_timeout {
                let elapsed = progress.last_progress.elapsed();
                hangs.push((name.clone(), child.generation, elapsed));
            }
        }

        for (name, generation, elapsed) in hangs {
            let _ = self.event_tx.send(SupervisorEvent::HangDetected {
                name: name.clone(),
                generation,
                elapsed,
            });

            if let Some(child) = self.children.get_mut(&name)
                && let Some(cancel) = child.child_cancel.take()
            {
                child.hung = true;
                cancel.cancel();
            }
        }
    }
}
```

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-03-28 23:40:03

```
use std::time::Duration;

use super::ChildExit;

/// Lifecycle events emitted by the supervisor via a `broadcast` channel.
///
/// Subscribe with [`SupervisorHandle::subscribe`](super::SupervisorHandle::subscribe)
/// to observe starts, stops, restarts, and hang detections.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub enum SupervisorEvent {
    /// The supervisor's event loop has started.
    SupervisorStarted,
    /// The supervisor is draining children before shutting down.
    SupervisorStopping,
    /// A child was spawned (or respawned) successfully.
    ChildStarted { name: String, generation: u64 },
    /// A child's run future completed.
    ChildExited {
        name: String,
        generation: u64,
        exit: ChildExit,
    },
    /// A child was restarted after a failure, with the backoff `delay` applied.
    ChildRestarted {
        name: String,
        old_gen: u64,
        new_gen: u64,
        delay: Duration,
    },
    /// A child has been busy without reporting progress longer than its timeout.
    HangDetected {
        name: String,
        generation: u64,
        elapsed: Duration,
    },
    /// A single child hit its per-child restart limit and will not be restarted again.
    ChildRestartLimitExceeded { name: String, restarts: u64 },
    /// Supervisor-wide restart intensity exceeded — the supervisor shuts down.
    RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts: u64 },
    /// A token budget was exceeded (reserved for future event-emitter wiring).
    BudgetExceeded { name: String, used: u64, limit: u64 },
}
```


### Tool Call [completed]: Read /Users/yuan/Developer/mra/src/supervisor/runner.rs

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-03-28 23:40:07

```
use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::sync::Arc;
use std::time::Duration;

use tokio::sync::{broadcast, mpsc, watch};
use tokio::task::JoinSet;
use tokio_util::sync::CancellationToken;

use crate::agent::AgentHandle;
use crate::agent::ProgressState;
use crate::agent::mailbox::MailboxSlot;
use crate::budget::BudgetTracker;
use crate::error::SupervisorError;
use crate::ids::AgentId;
use crate::tool::ToolRegistry;

use super::ChildExit;
use super::child::{ChildContext, ChildSpec};
use super::config::{ChildRestart, Strategy, SupervisorConfig};
use super::event::SupervisorEvent;
use super::handle::SupervisorCommand;
use super::tracker::{IntensityTracker, RestartTracker};

struct ChildState {
    spec: ChildSpec,
    id: AgentId,
    generation: u64,
    progress: Option<watch::Receiver<ProgressState>>,
    child_cancel: Option<CancellationToken>,
    mailbox: Arc<MailboxSlot>,
    logical_cancel: CancellationToken,
    tracker: RestartTracker,
    alive: bool,
    hung: bool,
}

pub(crate) struct SupervisorRunner {
    config: SupervisorConfig,
    children: HashMap<String, ChildState>,
    child_order: Vec<String>,
    task_map: HashMap<tokio::task::Id, String>,
    join_set: JoinSet<ChildExit>,
    command_rx: mpsc::Receiver<SupervisorCommand>,
    event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>,
    cancel: CancellationToken,
    intensity: IntensityTracker,
    budget: Option<Arc<BudgetTracker>>,
}

impl SupervisorRunner {
    pub(crate) fn new(
        config: SupervisorConfig,
        command_rx: mpsc::Receiver<SupervisorCommand>,
        event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>,
        budget: Option<Arc<BudgetTracker>>,
    ) -> Self {
        let intensity = IntensityTracker::new(config.intensity.clone());
        Self {
            config,
            children: HashMap::new(),
            child_order: Vec::new(),
            task_map: HashMap::new(),
            join_set: JoinSet::new(),
            command_rx,
            event_tx,
            cancel: CancellationToken::new(),
            intensity,
            budget,
        }
    }

    pub(crate) async fn run(mut self) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        let mut hang_tick = tokio::time::interval(self.config.hang_check_interval);
        hang_tick.set_missed_tick_behavior(tokio::time::MissedTickBehavior::Skip);

        self.emit(SupervisorEvent::SupervisorStarted);

        loop {
            tokio::select! {
                _ = self.cancel.cancelled() => {
                    self.drain_all().await;
                    break Ok(());
                }

                Some(result) = self.join_set.join_next_with_id() => {
                    self.handle_child_exit(result).await?;
                }

                cmd = self.command_rx.recv() => match cmd {
                    None => {
                        self.drain_all().await;
                        break Ok(());
                    }
                    Some(cmd) => self.handle_command(cmd).await?,
                },

                _ = hang_tick.tick() => {
                    self.check_hangs().await;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    fn emit(&self, event: SupervisorEvent) {
        let _ = self.event_tx.send(event);
    }

    async fn handle_command(&mut self, cmd: SupervisorCommand) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        match cmd {
            SupervisorCommand::StartChild { spec, reply } => {
                let result = self.do_start_child(spec).await;
                let _ = reply.send(result);
            }
            SupervisorCommand::StopChild { name, reply } => {
                let result = self.do_stop_child(&name).await;
                let _ = reply.send(result);
            }
            SupervisorCommand::GetChild { name, reply } => {
                let handle = self.children.get(&name).map(|child| {
                    AgentHandle::new(
                        child.id,
                        child.mailbox.clone(),
                        child.logical_cancel.clone(),
                    )
                });
                let _ = reply.send(handle);
            }
            SupervisorCommand::Shutdown => {
                self.drain_all().await;
                self.cancel.cancel();
            }
        }
        Ok(())
    }

    async fn do_start_child(&mut self, spec: ChildSpec) -> Result<AgentHandle, SupervisorError> {
        let name = spec.name.clone();
        let id = AgentId::new();
        let logical_cancel = CancellationToken::new();
        let child_cancel = logical_cancel.child_token();

        // Create stable mailbox with dummy sender
        let (dummy_tx, _) = mpsc::channel(1);
        let mailbox = Arc::new(MailboxSlot::new(dummy_tx));

        // Build peers map from existing alive children
        let peers: HashMap<String, AgentHandle> = self
            .children
            .iter()
            .filter(|(_, c)| c.alive)
            .map(|(n, c)| {
                (
                    n.clone(),
                    AgentHandle::new(c.id, c.mailbox.clone(), c.logical_cancel.clone()),
                )
            })
            .collect();

        // Register agent budget slot if budget tracking is active
        if let Some(ref budget) = self.budget {
            budget.register_agent(&name, spec.token_budget);
        }

        // Call factory
        let ctx = ChildContext {
            id,
            generation: 0,
            cancel: child_cancel.clone(),
            peers,
            llm: None,
            budget: self.budget.clone(),
            tools: ToolRegistry::new(),
        };
        let spawned = (spec.factory)(ctx)
            .await
            .map_err(|e| SupervisorError::SpawnFailed(e.to_string()))?;

        // Swap real sender into stable mailbox
        mailbox.swap(spawned.sender);

        // Build the stable handle
        let handle = AgentHandle::new(id, mailbox.clone(), logical_cancel.clone());

        // Spawn future in JoinSet
        let abort = self.join_set.spawn(spawned.future);
        let task_id = abort.id();
        self.task_map.insert(task_id, name.clone());

        let tracker = RestartTracker::new(&spec.config.restart_policy);

        let state = ChildState {
            spec,
            id,
            generation: 0,
            progress: Some(spawned.progress),
            child_cancel: Some(child_cancel),
            mailbox,
            logical_cancel,
            tracker,
            alive: true,
            hung: false,
        };

        self.children.insert(name.clone(), state);
        self.child_order.push(name.clone());

        self.emit(SupervisorEvent::ChildStarted {
            name,
            generation: 0,
        });

        Ok(handle)
    }

    async fn do_stop_child(&mut self, name: &str) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        let child = self
            .children
            .get_mut(name)
            .ok_or_else(|| SupervisorError::ChildNotFound(name.into()))?;

        if let Some(cancel) = child.child_cancel.take() {
            cancel.cancel();
        }
        child.alive = false;
        Ok(())
    }

    async fn handle_child_exit(
        &mut self,
        result: Result<(tokio::task::Id, ChildExit), tokio::task::JoinError>,
    ) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        let (task_id, exit) = match result {
            Ok((id, exit)) => (id, exit),
            Err(e) => {
                let id = e.id();
                (id, ChildExit::Failed(format!("task panicked: {e}")))
            }
        };

        let Some(name) = self.task_map.remove(&task_id) else {
            return Ok(());
        };

        let (old_gen, should_restart) = {
            let Some(child) = self.children.get_mut(&name) else {
                return Ok(());
            };

            let old_gen = child.generation;
            child.alive = false;
            child.child_cancel = None;
            child.progress = None;

            // Hung children exit with Shutdown, which isn't a "failure" —
            // override so Transient restart policy still kicks in.
            let is_failure = if child.hung {
                child.hung = false;
                true
            } else {
                exit.is_failure()
            };
            let should_restart = child.spec.restart.should_restart(is_failure);
            (old_gen, should_restart)
        };

        let _ = self.event_tx.send(SupervisorEvent::ChildExited {
            name: name.clone(),
            generation: old_gen,
            exit,
        });

        if !should_restart || self.cancel.is_cancelled() {
            return Ok(());
        }

        match self.config.strategy {
            Strategy::OneForOne => {
                // Record in per-child tracker
                let now = tokio::time::Instant::now();
                let child = self.children.get_mut(&name).unwrap();
                child.tracker.record(now);

                if child.tracker.exceeded() {
                    let restarts = child.tracker.total_restarts;
                    let _ = self
                        .event_tx
                        .send(SupervisorEvent::ChildRestartLimitExceeded { name, restarts });
                    return Ok(());
                }

                // Record in per-supervisor intensity tracker
                self.intensity.record(now);
                if self.intensity.exceeded() {
                    let total_restarts = self.intensity.total_restarts;
                    let _ = self
                        .event_tx
                        .send(SupervisorEvent::RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts });
                    self.drain_all().await;
                    return Err(SupervisorError::RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts });
                }

                // Compute backoff delay and sleep
                let child = self.children.get(&name).unwrap();
                let delay = child.tracker.backoff_delay();
                tokio::time::sleep(delay).await;

                // Don't restart if cancelled during backoff sleep
                if self.cancel.is_cancelled() {
                    return Ok(());
                }

                // Build peers map from alive siblings
                let peers: HashMap<String, AgentHandle> = self
                    .children
                    .iter()
                    .filter(|(n, c)| c.alive && *n != &name)
                    .map(|(n, c)| {
                        (
                            n.clone(),
                            AgentHandle::new(c.id, c.mailbox.clone(), c.logical_cancel.clone()),
                        )
                    })
                    .collect();

                let child = self.children.get_mut(&name).unwrap();

                // Increment generation and create new per-generation cancel token
                let new_gen = old_gen + 1;
                let child_cancel = child.logical_cancel.child_token();

                let ctx = ChildContext {
                    id: child.id,
                    generation: new_gen,
                    cancel: child_cancel.clone(),
                    peers,
                    llm: None,
                    budget: self.budget.clone(),
                    tools: ToolRegistry::new(),
                };

                let spawned = match (child.spec.factory)(ctx).await {
                    Ok(s) => s,
                    Err(_) => {
                        // Factory failed — leave child dead
                        return Ok(());
                    }
                };

                // Hot-swap sender into stable mailbox
                child.mailbox.swap(spawned.sender);

                // Spawn new future in JoinSet
                let abort = self.join_set.spawn(spawned.future);
                let new_task_id = abort.id();
                self.task_map.insert(new_task_id, name.clone());

                // Update child state
                child.generation = new_gen;
                child.progress = Some(spawned.progress);
                child.child_cancel = Some(child_cancel);
                child.alive = true;

                let _ = self.event_tx.send(SupervisorEvent::ChildRestarted {
                    name,
                    old_gen,
                    new_gen,
                    delay,
                });
            }
            Strategy::OneForAll => {
                self.restart_all(&name).await?;
            }
        }

        Ok(())
    }

    async fn restart_all(&mut self, trigger_name: &str) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        // 1. Cancel all alive children (except the one that already exited)
        for (name, child) in &self.children {
            if name != trigger_name
                && let Some(ref cancel) = child.child_cancel
            {
                cancel.cancel();
            }
        }

        // 2. Wait for all to exit
        while self.join_set.join_next().await.is_some() {}
        self.task_map.clear();

        // 3. Record restart in per-supervisor intensity tracker
        let now = tokio::time::Instant::now();
        self.intensity.record(now);
        if self.intensity.exceeded() {
            let total = self.intensity.total_restarts;
            let _ = self
                .event_tx
                .send(SupervisorEvent::RestartIntensityExceeded {
                    total_restarts: total,
                });
            self.drain_all().await;
            return Err(SupervisorError::RestartIntensityExceeded {
                total_restarts: total,
            });
        }

        // 4. Respawn all non-Temporary children in insertion order
        let order = self.child_order.clone();
        for child_name in &order {
            // Skip Temporary children
            {
                let child = self.children.get_mut(child_name).unwrap();
                if matches!(child.spec.restart, ChildRestart::Temporary) {
                    child.alive = false;
                    continue;
                }
            }

            if self.cancel.is_cancelled() {
                return Ok(());
            }

            let (old_gen, new_gen, child_cancel, child_id) = {
                let child = self.children.get(child_name).unwrap();
                let old_gen = child.generation;
                let new_gen = old_gen + 1;
                let child_cancel = child.logical_cancel.child_token();
                (old_gen, new_gen, child_cancel, child.id)
            };

            // Build peers from already-respawned siblings
            let peers: HashMap<String, AgentHandle> = self
                .children
                .iter()
                .filter(|(n, c)| c.alive && *n != child_name)
                .map(|(n, c)| {
                    (
                        n.clone(),
                        AgentHandle::new(c.id, c.mailbox.clone(), c.logical_cancel.clone()),
                    )
                })
                .collect();

            let child = self.children.get_mut(child_name).unwrap();
            let ctx = ChildContext {
                id: child_id,
                generation: new_gen,
                cancel: child_cancel.clone(),
                peers,
                llm: None,
                budget: self.budget.clone(),
                tools: ToolRegistry::new(),
            };

            let spawned = match (child.spec.factory)(ctx).await {
                Ok(s) => s,
                Err(_) => {
                    child.alive = false;
                    continue;
                }
            };

            child.mailbox.swap(spawned.sender);
            let abort = self.join_set.spawn(spawned.future);
            self.task_map.insert(abort.id(), child_name.clone());

            child.generation = new_gen;
            child.progress = Some(spawned.progress);
            child.child_cancel = Some(child_cancel);
            child.alive = true;
            child.tracker.record(now);

            let _ = self.event_tx.send(SupervisorEvent::ChildRestarted {
                name: child_name.clone(),
                old_gen,
                new_gen,
                delay: Duration::from_millis(0),
            });
        }

        Ok(())
    }

    async fn drain_all(&mut self) {
        self.emit(SupervisorEvent::SupervisorStopping);
        for child in self.children.values() {
            if let Some(ref cancel) = child.child_cancel {
                cancel.cancel();
            }
        }
        while self.join_set.join_next().await.is_some() {}
    }

    async fn check_hangs(&mut self) {
        let mut hangs = Vec::new();

        for (name, child) in &self.children {
            if !child.alive {
                continue;
            }
            let Some(hang_timeout) = child.spec.hang_timeout else {
                continue;
            };
            let Some(ref progress_rx) = child.progress else {
                continue;
            };

            let progress = progress_rx.borrow();
            if progress.busy && progress.last_progress.elapsed() > hang_timeout {
                let elapsed = progress.last_progress.elapsed();
                hangs.push((name.clone(), child.generation, elapsed));
            }
        }

        for (name, generation, elapsed) in hangs {
            let _ = self.event_tx.send(SupervisorEvent::HangDetected {
                name: name.clone(),
                generation,
                elapsed,
            });

            if let Some(child) = self.children.get_mut(&name)
                && let Some(cancel) = child.child_cancel.take()
            {
                child.hung = true;
                cancel.cancel();
            }
        }
    }
}

**Tool:** search

```
use std::time::Duration;

use super::ChildExit;

/// Lifecycle events emitted by the supervisor via a `broadcast` channel.
///
/// Subscribe with [`SupervisorHandle::subscribe`](super::SupervisorHandle::subscribe)
/// to observe starts, stops, restarts, and hang detections.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub enum SupervisorEvent {
    /// The supervisor's event loop has started.
    SupervisorStarted,
    /// The supervisor is draining children before shutting down.
    SupervisorStopping,
    /// A child was spawned (or respawned) successfully.
    ChildStarted { name: String, generation: u64 },
    /// A child's run future completed.
    ChildExited {
        name: String,
        generation: u64,
        exit: ChildExit,
    },
    /// A child was restarted after a failure, with the backoff `delay` applied.
    ChildRestarted {
        name: String,
        old_gen: u64,
        new_gen: u64,
        delay: Duration,
    },
    /// A child has been busy without reporting progress longer than its timeout.
    HangDetected {
        name: String,
        generation: u64,
        elapsed: Duration,
    },
    /// A single child hit its per-child restart limit and will not be restarted again.
    ChildRestartLimitExceeded { name: String, restarts: u64 },
    /// Supervisor-wide restart intensity exceeded — the supervisor shuts down.
    RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts: u64 },
    /// A token budget was exceeded (reserved for future event-emitter wiring).
    BudgetExceeded { name: String, used: u64, limit: u64 },
}
```


### Tool Call [completed]: Design minimal RestartManager

**Description:** Design minimal RestartManager

```
Now I have a complete picture of the restart system. Let me design a minimal RestartManager interface.

---

## RestartManager Interface Design

### 1. Interface Signature

```rust
use std::time::Duration;
use tokio::time::Instant;

/// Single-responsibility restart coordinator.
///
/// Decides synchronously whether restart should happen, tracks all limits,
/// and returns async delay instructions (never blocks).
pub struct RestartManager {
    config: RestartConfig,
    child_trackers: HashMap<String, RestartTracker>,
    intensity: IntensityTracker,
    event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>,
}

/// Configuration injected at construction.
pub struct RestartConfig {
    pub strategy: Strategy,
    pub intensity: RestartIntensity,
}

/// What the manager decided.
pub enum RestartDecision {
    /// Restart this child after the specified delay.
    Restart { delay: Duration },
    /// Restart all children (no individual delays; OneForAll).
    RestartAll,
    /// Don't restart — policy says no.
    Skip,
    /// Don't restart — per-child limit exceeded.
    ChildLimitExceeded { restarts: u64 },
    /// Don't restart — global intensity exceeded; shut down supervisor.
    IntensityExceeded { total_restarts: u64 },
}

impl RestartManager {
    /// **THE ONLY ENTRY POINT**
    ///
    /// Called by supervisor when a child exits. Returns a synchronous decision.
    /// Supervisor interprets the decision and applies delays/cascades.
    pub fn decide(
        &mut self,
        child_name: &str,
        exit: &ChildExit,
        policy: &ChildRestart,
        was_hung: bool,
    ) -> RestartDecision {
        // 1. Check if restart policy says to restart
        let is_failure = was_hung || exit.is_failure();
        if !policy.should_restart(is_failure) {
            self.emit(SupervisorEvent::ChildExited { ... });
            return RestartDecision::Skip;
        }

        let now = Instant::now();

        // 2. Strategy-specific logic
        match self.config.strategy {
            Strategy::OneForOne => {
                // Get or create per-child tracker
                let tracker = self.child_trackers
                    .entry(child_name.to_string())
                    .or_insert_with(|| RestartTracker::new(policy));

                // Record restart in per-child tracker
                tracker.record(now);

                // Check per-child limit
                if tracker.exceeded() {
                    let restarts = tracker.total_restarts;
                    self.emit(SupervisorEvent::ChildRestartLimitExceeded {
                        name: child_name.into(),
                        restarts,
                    });
                    return RestartDecision::ChildLimitExceeded { restarts };
                }

                // Record in global intensity tracker
                self.intensity.record(now);

                // Check global intensity
                if self.intensity.exceeded() {
                    let total = self.intensity.total_restarts;
                    self.emit(SupervisorEvent::RestartIntensityExceeded {
                        total_restarts: total,
                    });
                    return RestartDecision::IntensityExceeded { total_restarts: total };
                }

                // Compute backoff delay
                let delay = tracker.backoff_delay();
                RestartDecision::Restart { delay }
            }
            Strategy::OneForAll => {
                // Record in global intensity only (no per-child tracking for OneForAll)
                self.intensity.record(now);

                if self.intensity.exceeded() {
                    let total = self.intensity.total_restarts;
                    self.emit(SupervisorEvent::RestartIntensityExceeded {
                        total_restarts: total,
                    });
                    return RestartDecision::IntensityExceeded { total_restarts: total };
                }

                RestartDecision::RestartAll
            }
        }
    }

    /// Internal event emitter.
    fn emit(&self, event: SupervisorEvent) {
        let _ = self.event_tx.send(event);
    }
}
```

---

### 2. Usage Example

**Before (scattered across runner.rs, ~100 LOC):**

```rust
// In handle_child_exit, manual inline logic:
if !should_restart || self.cancel.is_cancelled() { return Ok(()); }
match self.config.strategy {
    Strategy::OneForOne => {
        let child = self.children.get_mut(&name).unwrap();
        child.tracker.record(now);
        if child.tracker.exceeded() { ... emit event ... return Ok(()); }
        self.intensity.record(now);
        if self.intensity.exceeded() { ... emit ... drain_all ... return Err(...); }
        let delay = child.tracker.backoff_delay();
        tokio::time::sleep(delay).await;  // BLOCKS SUPERVISOR LOOP
        // ... restart logic ...
    }
    Strategy::OneForAll => { ... 50 more lines ... }
}
```

**After (single call site):**

```rust
async fn handle_child_exit(&mut self, task_id: Id, exit: ChildExit) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
    let Some(name) = self.task_map.remove(&task_id) else { return Ok(()); };

    let (was_hung, policy, old_gen) = {
        let child = self.children.get_mut(&name)?;
        child.alive = false;
        child.child_cancel = None;
        (child.hung, child.spec.restart, child.generation)
    };

    // **THE ONLY CALL TO RestartManager**
    let decision = self.restart_mgr.decide(&name, &exit, &policy, was_hung);

    match decision {
        RestartDecision::Skip => Ok(()),

        RestartDecision::Restart { delay } => {
            // Spawn async delay task (non-blocking)
            let name = name.clone();
            let restart_tx = self.restart_tx.clone();
            tokio::spawn(async move {
                tokio::time::sleep(delay).await;
                let _ = restart_tx.send(RestartCommand::RestartChild { name, old_gen }).await;
            });
            Ok(())
        }

        RestartDecision::RestartAll => {
            self.handle_restart_all(&name).await?;
            Ok(())
        }

        RestartDecision::ChildLimitExceeded { .. } => Ok(()),

        RestartDecision::IntensityExceeded { total_restarts } => {
            self.drain_all().await;
            Err(SupervisorError::RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts })
        }
    }
}
```

**New async loop to apply delayed restarts:**

```rust
// In run() select loop, add branch:
restart_cmd = self.restart_rx.recv() => match restart_cmd {
    Some(RestartCommand::RestartChild { name, old_gen }) => {
        // Check still dead and generation matches (race protection)
        if let Some(child) = self.children.get(&name)
            && !child.alive
            && child.generation == old_gen
            && !self.cancel.is_cancelled()
        {
            self.do_restart_child(&name).await?;
        }
    }
    None => {} // channel closed
}
```

---

### 3. Complexity Hidden Internally

**What the interface hides:**

1. **Dual tracker coordination**: Switches between per-child (OneForOne) vs global-only (OneForAll).
2. **Hung child override**: `was_hung` flag converts `ChildExit::Shutdown` → failure for Transient policy.
3. **Exponential backoff calculation**: `tracker.backoff_delay()` encapsulated.
4. **Event emission**: All `SupervisorEvent` emissions happen inside `decide()`.
5. **Tracker lifecycle**: Lazy creation of per-child trackers (`entry().or_insert_with()`).
6. **Intensity failure short-circuit**: Global intensity checked **after** per-child for OneForOne.
7. **Policy logic**: `ChildRestart::should_restart(is_failure)` centralized.

**What the supervisor still owns:**

- Spawning delayed restart tasks (supervisor decides *how* to delay).
- Cascading logic for `RestartAll` (coordinator just signals the decision).
- Child state management (alive/dead, generation counter).
- Actual respawn logic (factory call, mailbox swap, JoinSet spawn).

---

### 4. Dependency Strategy

**Injected (constructor dependencies):**

```rust
impl RestartManager {
    pub fn new(
        config: RestartConfig,
        event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>,
    ) -> Self {
        Self {
            config,
            child_trackers: HashMap::new(),
            intensity: IntensityTracker::new(config.intensity.clone()),
            event_tx,
        }
    }
}
```

**Why this split:**

- **Event sender**: Supervisor owns the broadcast channel; manager borrows sender to emit events.
- **Strategy/intensity config**: Immutable config passed once at construction.
- **Child trackers**: Manager owns the `HashMap<String, RestartTracker>` — supervisor doesn't need per-child state.

**What it does NOT depend on:**

- `ChildState` struct (supervisor's internal state).
- `JoinSet` or `task_map` (spawn mechanics).
- Tokio sleep/timers (decision is synchronous; supervisor applies delay).

---

### 5. Trade-offs

#### **GAINS**

1. **Single responsibility**: Restart *decision* isolated from *execution*.
2. **Non-blocking backoff**: Supervisor loop never blocks — delays spawn async tasks.
3. **Testable in isolation**: Mock `event_tx`, inject fake `Instant::now()` for tests.
4. **Clear contract**: `RestartDecision` enum makes all outcomes explicit (no hidden side effects).
5. **100 LOC reduction**: Eliminates inline branching, tracker fiddling, event emission from runner.rs.
6. **Reusable**: Other supervisor strategies (e.g., `RestForOne`) just add enum variants.

#### **LOSSES**

1. **Indirection cost**: One extra enum allocation per child exit (negligible).
2. **Split restart flow**: Supervisor must interpret `RestartDecision` and spawn delay tasks (5-10 LOC overhead).
3. **No async in `decide()`**: Can't consult async oracles (e.g., external rate limiter). Workaround: pre-fetch before calling `decide()`.
4. **Restart command channel**: New `mpsc` for delayed restart messages (1 extra select branch).

#### **Alternative: 2-method interface**

If you wanted to split backoff from decision:

```rust
pub fn should_restart(&mut self, ...) -> RestartOutcome;
pub fn compute_delay(&self, child_name: &str) -> Duration;
```

**Why I reject this:**

- Forces supervisor to track state ("did I already call `should_restart`?").
- Breaks atomicity (what if child limit exceeded *after* computing delay?).
- Still 2 entry points (not minimal).

---

### 6. Key Design Insight

**The "Aha!" moment:**

> **Restart decisions are synchronous; backoff delays are asynchronous.**

By separating *what to do* (synchronous enum) from *when to do it* (async spawn), we:

- Keep the supervisor loop unblocked.
- Maintain tracker state synchronously (no Arc/Mutex).
- Emit events at decision time (not later).
- Allow cancellation during backoff (check `generation` before restart).

**The minimal interface is not "fewer methods" — it's "the right split of concerns."**

---

### Summary Table

| Aspect | Current (scattered) | RestartManager (minimal) |
|--------|---------------------|--------------------------|
| **Entry points** | Inline in `handle_child_exit` | 1 method: `decide()` |
| **Blocking** | `tokio::time::sleep` blocks loop | Async task spawned |
| **Testability** | Mock entire supervisor | Mock event sender + inject trackers |
| **LOC** | ~150 in runner.rs | ~50 in manager, ~30 in supervisor glue |
| **Cascades** | Inline `restart_all()` | `RestartDecision::RestartAll` signal |
| **Event emission** | Scattered (6 sites) | Centralized in `decide()` |

Perfect! Now I have a complete picture. Let me design a RestartManager interface optimized for the 80% use case.

---

## RestartManager Interface Design

### 1. Interface Signature

```rust
use std::time::Duration;
use tokio::time::Instant;

/// Decision returned by RestartManager — tells supervisor what to do next.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub enum RestartDecision {
    /// Restart this child after the specified delay.
    RestartAfter { delay: Duration },
    /// Restart all children in order (OneForAll cascade).
    RestartAll,
    /// Don't restart — child exceeded its limit.
    ChildLimitExceeded { restarts: u64 },
    /// Don't restart — supervisor-wide intensity exceeded (fatal).
    IntensityExceeded { total_restarts: u64 },
    /// Don't restart — policy says no (Temporary, or Transient+Normal exit).
    NoRestart,
}

/// The 80% use case: decide if/how to restart a crashed child.
/// Hides both per-child and global tracking, policy evaluation, and backoff calculation.
pub struct RestartManager {
    strategy: Strategy,
    children: HashMap<String, ChildRestartState>,
    intensity: IntensityTracker,
}

struct ChildRestartState {
    policy: ChildRestart,
    tracker: RestartTracker,
}

impl RestartManager {
    /// Creates a new RestartManager with supervisor-wide config.
    pub fn new(config: SupervisorConfig) -> Self {
        Self {
            strategy: config.strategy,
            children: HashMap::new(),
            intensity: IntensityTracker::new(config.intensity),
        }
    }

    /// Registers a child for restart tracking. Call once on initial start.
    pub fn register(&mut self, name: &str, spec: &ChildSpec) {
        self.children.insert(
            name.to_owned(),
            ChildRestartState {
                policy: spec.restart,
                tracker: RestartTracker::new(&spec.config.restart_policy),
            },
        );
    }

    /// The one-liner: "This child exited — what should I do?"
    ///
    /// Synchronously decides whether to restart, checking:
    /// - Restart policy (Permanent/Transient/Temporary)
    /// - Per-child restart limits
    /// - Supervisor-wide intensity limits
    /// - OneForOne vs OneForAll strategy
    ///
    /// Returns a decision with computed backoff delay (if applicable).
    /// **Does NOT sleep** — supervisor must schedule the delay.
    pub fn decide(
        &mut self,
        name: &str,
        exit: &ChildExit,
        now: Instant,
    ) -> RestartDecision {
        let Some(child) = self.children.get_mut(name) else {
            return RestartDecision::NoRestart;
        };

        // 1. Evaluate restart policy
        if !child.policy.should_restart(exit.is_failure()) {
            return RestartDecision::NoRestart;
        }

        // 2. Record restart timestamp
        child.tracker.record(now);

        // 3. Check per-child limit
        if child.tracker.exceeded() {
            return RestartDecision::ChildLimitExceeded {
                restarts: child.tracker.total_restarts,
            };
        }

        // 4. Record in global intensity tracker
        self.intensity.record(now);

        // 5. Check supervisor-wide intensity
        if self.intensity.exceeded() {
            return RestartDecision::IntensityExceeded {
                total_restarts: self.intensity.total_restarts,
            };
        }

        // 6. Apply strategy
        match self.strategy {
            Strategy::OneForOne => {
                let delay = child.tracker.backoff_delay();
                RestartDecision::RestartAfter { delay }
            }
            Strategy::OneForAll => RestartDecision::RestartAll,
        }
    }

    /// For OneForAll: records restart for all children except Temporary.
    /// Call AFTER canceling all children, BEFORE respawning.
    pub fn record_all(&mut self, now: Instant) {
        for child in self.children.values_mut() {
            if !matches!(child.policy, ChildRestart::Temporary) {
                child.tracker.record(now);
            }
        }
    }

    /// Returns current backoff delay for a child (useful for OneForAll ordering).
    pub fn backoff_delay(&self, name: &str) -> Duration {
        self.children
            .get(name)
            .map(|c| c.tracker.backoff_delay())
            .unwrap_or_default()
    }

    /// Removes a child from tracking (on explicit stop).
    pub fn unregister(&mut self, name: &str) {
        self.children.remove(name);
    }
}
```

### 2. Usage Example: Supervisor Calls It

**Before (scattered across 100+ lines in runner.rs):**
```rust
// Inside handle_child_exit — interleaved with mailbox swaps, peer builds, etc.
let is_failure = if child.hung { true } else { exit.is_failure() };
let should_restart = child.spec.restart.should_restart(is_failure);
if !should_restart { return Ok(()); }

match self.config.strategy {
    Strategy::OneForOne => {
        let now = Instant::now();
        child.tracker.record(now);
        if child.tracker.exceeded() { /* emit event, return */ }
        self.intensity.record(now);
        if self.intensity.exceeded() { /* drain all, error */ }
        let delay = child.tracker.backoff_delay();
        tokio::time::sleep(delay).await;  // BLOCKS SUPERVISOR LOOP!
        // ... spawn logic ...
    }
    Strategy::OneForAll => { /* 50 more lines */ }
}
```

**After (10 lines in supervisor loop):**
```rust
async fn handle_child_exit(&mut self, task_id: tokio::task::Id, exit: ChildExit) {
    let Some(name) = self.task_map.remove(&task_id) else { return Ok(()) };
    
    // Mark child as dead, emit exit event
    self.mark_child_exited(&name, exit.clone());

    // ONE-LINER: decide what to do
    let decision = self.restart_mgr.decide(&name, &exit, Instant::now());

    match decision {
        RestartDecision::NoRestart => Ok(()),
        
        RestartDecision::RestartAfter { delay } => {
            // Schedule delayed restart (non-blocking)
            let name = name.clone();
            let when = Instant::now() + delay;
            self.pending_restarts.push(PendingRestart { name, when });
            Ok(())
        }
        
        RestartDecision::RestartAll => {
            self.cascade_restart_all().await
        }
        
        RestartDecision::ChildLimitExceeded { restarts } => {
            self.emit(SupervisorEvent::ChildRestartLimitExceeded { name, restarts });
            Ok(())
        }
        
        RestartDecision::IntensityExceeded { total_restarts } => {
            self.emit(SupervisorEvent::RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts });
            self.drain_all().await;
            Err(SupervisorError::RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts })
        }
    }
}
```

**Supervisor loop now handles backoff non-blockingly:**
```rust
loop {
    tokio::select! {
        _ = self.cancel.cancelled() => { /* ... */ }
        
        Some(result) = self.join_set.join_next_with_id() => {
            self.handle_child_exit(result).await?;
        }
        
        // NEW: poll pending restarts (no sleep!)
        _ = self.next_restart_ready(), if !self.pending_restarts.is_empty() => {
            let restart = self.pending_restarts.pop().unwrap();
            self.spawn_child(&restart.name).await?;
        }
        
        cmd = self.command_rx.recv() => { /* ... */ }
        _ = hang_tick.tick() => { /* ... */ }
    }
}

async fn next_restart_ready(&self) -> Instant {
    self.pending_restarts
        .iter()
        .map(|r| r.when)
        .min()
        .unwrap_or_else(|| Instant::now() + Duration::from_secs(3600))
}
```

### 3. Complexity Hidden Internally

**What the interface encapsulates:**
1. **Dual tracking**: Per-child `RestartTracker` + global `IntensityTracker` coordinated in one call
2. **Sliding window eviction**: Old timestamps pruned automatically on `record()`
3. **Exponential backoff math**: `2^n * base_delay`, capped at `max_delay`
4. **Policy evaluation logic**: Permanent/Transient/Temporary + exit type checks
5. **Strategy dispatch**: OneForOne vs OneForAll branching
6. **Hung child override**: Caller can mark exit as failure even if it's `Shutdown`
7. **State management**: HashMap of per-child trackers, insertion order preserved externally

**What it deliberately DOESN'T hide:**
- Backoff delay scheduling (supervisor owns event loop timing)
- Spawning children (supervisor owns `JoinSet`, mailbox, peer wiring)
- Event emission (supervisor owns `broadcast::Sender`)
- OneForAll cascade ordering (supervisor knows child insertion order)

### 4. Dependency Strategy

**What RestartManager owns:**
- `HashMap<String, ChildRestartState>` — per-child policy + tracker
- `IntensityTracker` — supervisor-wide rate limiter
- `Strategy` — OneForOne vs OneForAll routing

**What it needs injected:**
- `SupervisorConfig` at construction (strategy + intensity config)
- `ChildSpec` at registration (per-child policy + restart policy)
- `Instant::now()` on each decision (testable, no hidden `Instant::now()` calls)

**What it does NOT depend on:**
- Tokio runtime (no `sleep`, no `spawn`)
- Event bus (no `broadcast::Sender`)
- Child state (`ChildState`, `JoinSet`, mailbox, peers) — that's supervisor's job
- External timers or priority queues

**Rationale:**
- **Testable**: Mock time by passing different `Instant` values
- **Portable**: Pure logic, no I/O — can extract to separate crate
- **Composable**: Supervisor decides how to act on `RestartDecision`

### 5. Trade-offs

| **Gain** | **Lose** |
|----------|----------|
| **80% case is 1 line**: `restart_mgr.decide(name, exit, now)` returns everything supervisor needs | Supervisor still schedules delays (but gains flexibility: can prioritize, cancel, batch) |
| **Synchronous decision**: No `await`, no blocking, supervisor loop stays responsive | OneForAll cascade still requires supervisor to cancel/wait/respawn (but that's inherent complexity) |
| **Testable in isolation**: Inject mock time, assert on `RestartDecision` enum | Supervisor must wire up `PendingRestart` queue + `select!` arm (one-time cost) |
| **No hidden state**: All tracking lives in `RestartManager`, easy to inspect/debug | Supervisor must call `register()` on child start (but it already tracks children) |
| **Type-safe decisions**: Enum forces handling all cases (limits, intensity, no-restart) | Can't hide event emission inside `decide()` — caller must match and emit (but events are context-dependent) |
| **Strategy-agnostic**: OneForOne returns delay, OneForAll returns cascade signal — same interface | OneForAll still needs `record_all()` helper (but explicit is better than magic) |
| **Backoff never blocks**: Delay is returned, not awaited — supervisor can cancel/preempt | Supervisor complexity shifts from "inline logic" to "state machine" (but gains control) |

**Key insight:**
The current code has **two problems**:
1. Restart logic is tangled with spawn/mailbox/peer logic (solved by extracting decision)
2. Backoff blocks the supervisor loop (solved by returning delay instead of sleeping)

This design solves both while keeping the common case trivial.

---

## Summary

**The 80% caller (OneForOne, default policy) writes:**
```rust
match restart_mgr.decide(&name, &exit, Instant::now()) {
    RestartDecision::RestartAfter { delay } => {
        self.schedule_restart(name, delay);
    }
    _ => { /* emit events, handle edge cases */ }
}
```

**The interface makes restart decisions synchronous, deterministic, and testable** while pushing delay scheduling back to the supervisor's event loop. This unblocks the loop and keeps restart logic pure.

agentId: a074ef1 (for resuming to continue this agent's work if needed)
```
