## RestartManager Interface Design

Based on my analysis of the codebase (runner.rs, tracker.rs, config.rs), I'll design a flexible, extensible RestartManager that maximizes configurability while maintaining the key constraints.

### 1. Interface Signature

```rust
use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::sync::Arc;
use std::time::Duration;
use tokio::time::Instant;

// ============================================================================
// Core Traits: Extension Points for Maximum Flexibility
// ============================================================================

/// Pluggable restart decision strategy.
/// 
/// Implementors decide whether a child should restart based on policy,
/// exit reason, and current state. This is synchronous by design.
pub trait RestartPolicy: Send + Sync {
    /// Returns true if the child should be restarted.
    fn should_restart(&self, exit: &ChildExit, hung: bool) -> bool;
}

/// Pluggable backoff algorithm.
/// 
/// Given the current restart history, compute the next delay duration.
/// This allows exponential, linear, jitter, or custom strategies.
pub trait BackoffStrategy: Send + Sync {
    /// Compute delay before next restart attempt.
    fn compute_delay(&self, history: &RestartHistory) -> Duration;
}

/// Pluggable limit checker for restart frequency.
/// 
/// Tracks restart attempts and returns whether the limit is exceeded.
/// Enables sliding windows, fixed counts, rate limiting, etc.
pub trait RestartLimiter: Send + Sync {
    /// Record a restart event at the given instant.
    fn record(&mut self, now: Instant);
    
    /// Returns true if the restart limit has been exceeded.
    fn exceeded(&self) -> bool;
    
    /// Returns restart count (for diagnostics).
    fn count(&self) -> u64;
}

/// Pluggable supervisor-wide restart strategy.
/// 
/// Decides which children to restart when one fails. Allows OneForOne,
/// OneForAll, RestForOne, dynamic dependency-based restarts, etc.
pub trait SupervisorStrategy: Send + Sync {
    /// Given a crashed child, return the list of children to restart (in order).
    /// 
    /// The list may include the crashed child itself, or exclude it if the
    /// strategy decides to abandon it. The returned names preserve insertion
    /// order for OneForAll-style cascades.
    fn select_targets<'a>(
        &self,
        crashed: &str,
        all_children: &'a [String],
        states: &HashMap<String, &ChildMetadata>,
    ) -> Vec<&'a str>;
}

/// Pluggable event emission strategy.
/// 
/// Allows users to customize what gets logged/emitted during restarts.
pub trait RestartObserver: Send + Sync {
    fn on_restart_decision(&self, child: &str, decision: RestartDecision);
    fn on_backoff_start(&self, child: &str, delay: Duration);
    fn on_limit_exceeded(&self, context: LimitContext);
}

// ============================================================================
// Data Types
// ============================================================================

/// Immutable snapshot of a child's restart history.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct RestartHistory {
    /// Recent restart timestamps (in sliding window).
    pub timestamps: Vec<Instant>,
    /// Total restarts since child was added (survives window evictions).
    pub total_restarts: u64,
    /// Current generation number.
    pub generation: u64,
}

/// Metadata about a child, passed to strategy implementations.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ChildMetadata {
    pub alive: bool,
    pub generation: u64,
    pub restart_policy: Arc<dyn RestartPolicy>,
}

/// Result of a restart decision.
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
pub enum RestartDecision {
    Restart,
    Abandon,
}

/// Context for limit-exceeded events.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub enum LimitContext {
    PerChild { name: String, count: u64 },
    Global { count: u64 },
}

/// Configuration for a child's restart behavior.
#[derive(Clone)]
pub struct ChildRestartConfig {
    pub policy: Arc<dyn RestartPolicy>,
    pub backoff: Arc<dyn BackoffStrategy>,
    pub limiter: Box<dyn RestartLimiter>,
}

/// Configuration for supervisor-wide restart management.
pub struct RestartManagerConfig {
    pub strategy: Arc<dyn SupervisorStrategy>,
    pub global_limiter: Box<dyn RestartLimiter>,
    pub observer: Arc<dyn RestartObserver>,
}

// ============================================================================
// Main Interface
// ============================================================================

/// Coordinates restart decisions, backoff scheduling, and limit enforcement.
/// 
/// This is the entry point that the supervisor loop calls when a child exits.
/// It hides all restart logic complexity while exposing maximum flexibility
/// through trait-based extension points.
pub struct RestartManager {
    config: RestartManagerConfig,
    child_configs: HashMap<String, ChildRestartConfig>,
    child_histories: HashMap<String, RestartHistory>,
}

/// Result of evaluating a child exit event.
pub struct RestartPlan {
    /// Children to restart, in order. Each entry includes the target name
    /// and the computed backoff delay for that specific child.
    pub targets: Vec<(String, Duration)>,
    
    /// If Some, a limit was exceeded and the supervisor should terminate.
    pub limit_exceeded: Option<LimitContext>,
}

impl RestartManager {
    /// Create a new restart manager with the given configuration.
    pub fn new(config: RestartManagerConfig) -> Self {
        Self {
            config,
            child_configs: HashMap::new(),
            child_histories: HashMap::new(),
        }
    }
    
    /// Register a new child with its restart configuration.
    pub fn add_child(&mut self, name: String, config: ChildRestartConfig) {
        self.child_histories.insert(
            name.clone(),
            RestartHistory {
                timestamps: Vec::new(),
                total_restarts: 0,
                generation: 0,
            },
        );
        self.child_configs.insert(name, config);
    }
    
    /// Remove a child from tracking (called when child is stopped).
    pub fn remove_child(&mut self, name: &str) {
        self.child_configs.remove(name);
        self.child_histories.remove(name);
    }
    
    /// Main decision point: analyze a child exit and produce a restart plan.
    /// 
    /// This is **synchronous** — it decides immediately what to do. The
    /// supervisor is responsible for spawning backoff sleeps as futures.
    pub fn evaluate_exit(
        &mut self,
        child_name: &str,
        exit: &ChildExit,
        hung: bool,
        child_order: &[String],
        child_metadata: &HashMap<String, ChildMetadata>,
    ) -> RestartPlan {
        let Some(child_config) = self.child_configs.get(child_name) else {
            return RestartPlan {
                targets: vec![],
                limit_exceeded: None,
            };
        };
        
        // Step 1: Consult restart policy (Permanent/Transient/Temporary)
        let should_restart = child_config.policy.should_restart(exit, hung);
        
        let decision = if should_restart {
            RestartDecision::Restart
        } else {
            RestartDecision::Abandon
        };
        
        self.config.observer.on_restart_decision(child_name, decision);
        
        if !should_restart {
            return RestartPlan {
                targets: vec![],
                limit_exceeded: None,
            };
        }
        
        // Step 2: Select targets based on supervisor strategy (OneForOne/OneForAll/etc)
        let targets = self.config.strategy.select_targets(
            child_name,
            child_order,
            child_metadata,
        );
        
        if targets.is_empty() {
            return RestartPlan {
                targets: vec![],
                limit_exceeded: None,
            };
        }
        
        // Step 3: Check global limit BEFORE recording anything
        let now = Instant::now();
        self.config.global_limiter.record(now);
        
        if self.config.global_limiter.exceeded() {
            let count = self.config.global_limiter.count();
            self.config.observer.on_limit_exceeded(LimitContext::Global { count });
            return RestartPlan {
                targets: vec![],
                limit_exceeded: Some(LimitContext::Global { count }),
            };
        }
        
        // Step 4: For each target, check per-child limit and compute backoff
        let mut plan_targets = Vec::new();
        
        for &target_name in &targets {
            let Some(target_config) = self.child_configs.get(target_name) else {
                continue;
            };
            
            let history = self.child_histories
                .entry(target_name.to_string())
                .or_insert_with(|| RestartHistory {
                    timestamps: Vec::new(),
                    total_restarts: 0,
                    generation: 0,
                });
            
            // Record restart in per-child limiter
            target_config.limiter.record(now);
            
            // Check per-child limit
            if target_config.limiter.exceeded() {
                let count = target_config.limiter.count();
                self.config.observer.on_limit_exceeded(LimitContext::PerChild {
                    name: target_name.to_string(),
                    count,
                });
                continue; // Skip this child, but continue with others
            }
            
            // Update history timestamps for backoff calculation
            history.timestamps.push(now);
            history.total_restarts += 1;
            
            // Compute backoff delay
            let delay = target_config.backoff.compute_delay(history);
            self.config.observer.on_backoff_start(target_name, delay);
            
            plan_targets.push((target_name.to_string(), delay));
        }
        
        RestartPlan {
            targets: plan_targets,
            limit_exceeded: None,
        }
    }
    
    /// Update the generation number for a child (called after successful restart).
    pub fn increment_generation(&mut self, name: &str) {
        if let Some(history) = self.child_histories.get_mut(name) {
            history.generation += 1;
        }
    }
    
    /// Get current restart history for a child (for diagnostics/metrics).
    pub fn history(&self, name: &str) -> Option<&RestartHistory> {
        self.child_histories.get(name)
    }
}

// ============================================================================
// Standard Implementations (Batteries Included)
// ============================================================================

/// Standard restart policies matching Erlang/OTP semantics.
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
pub enum StandardRestartPolicy {
    Permanent,
    Transient,
    Temporary,
}

impl RestartPolicy for StandardRestartPolicy {
    fn should_restart(&self, exit: &ChildExit, hung: bool) -> bool {
        // Hung children always treated as failures
        let is_failure = hung || exit.is_failure();
        
        match self {
            Self::Permanent => true,
            Self::Transient => is_failure,
            Self::Temporary => false,
        }
    }
}

/// Exponential backoff with configurable base and max.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ExponentialBackoff {
    pub base: Duration,
    pub max: Duration,
}

impl BackoffStrategy for ExponentialBackoff {
    fn compute_delay(&self, history: &RestartHistory) -> Duration {
        let n = history.timestamps.len().saturating_sub(1) as u32;
        let delay = self.base.saturating_mul(2u32.pow(n));
        delay.min(self.max)
    }
}

/// Sliding window restart limiter (Erlang/OTP style).
#[derive(Debug)]
pub struct SlidingWindowLimiter {
    timestamps: Vec<Instant>,
    max_restarts: u32,
    window: Duration,
    total: u64,
}

impl SlidingWindowLimiter {
    pub fn new(max_restarts: u32, window: Duration) -> Self {
        Self {
            timestamps: Vec::new(),
            max_restarts,
            window,
            total: 0,
        }
    }
}

impl RestartLimiter for SlidingWindowLimiter {
    fn record(&mut self, now: Instant) {
        self.total += 1;
        self.timestamps.push(now);
        
        // Evict old timestamps outside window
        let cutoff = now - self.window;
        self.timestamps.retain(|&t| t >= cutoff);
    }
    
    fn exceeded(&self) -> bool {
        self.timestamps.len() > self.max_restarts as usize
    }
    
    fn count(&self) -> u64 {
        self.total
    }
}

/// OneForOne: restart only the crashed child.
pub struct OneForOneStrategy;

impl SupervisorStrategy for OneForOneStrategy {
    fn select_targets<'a>(
        &self,
        crashed: &str,
        _all_children: &'a [String],
        _states: &HashMap<String, &ChildMetadata>,
    ) -> Vec<&'a str> {
        vec![crashed]
    }
}

/// OneForAll: restart all children when any one crashes.
pub struct OneForAllStrategy;

impl SupervisorStrategy for OneForAllStrategy {
    fn select_targets<'a>(
        &self,
        _crashed: &str,
        all_children: &'a [String],
        states: &HashMap<String, &ChildMetadata>,
    ) -> Vec<&'a str> {
        // Return all children except Temporary ones
        all_children
            .iter()
            .filter(|name| {
                states
                    .get(name.as_str())
                    .map(|meta| {
                        // Check if policy is not Temporary
                        // (This is pseudocode; actual implementation would need downcasting
                        // or a separate flag in ChildMetadata)
                        true
                    })
                    .unwrap_or(false)
            })
            .map(|s| s.as_str())
            .collect()
    }
}

/// No-op observer (silent mode).
pub struct SilentObserver;

impl RestartObserver for SilentObserver {
    fn on_restart_decision(&self, _child: &str, _decision: RestartDecision) {}
    fn on_backoff_start(&self, _child: &str, _delay: Duration) {}
    fn on_limit_exceeded(&self, _context: LimitContext) {}
}

/// Event-emitting observer (integrates with broadcast channel).
pub struct EventEmittingObserver {
    tx: tokio::sync::broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>,
}

impl EventEmittingObserver {
    pub fn new(tx: tokio::sync::broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>) -> Self {
        Self { tx }
    }
}

impl RestartObserver for EventEmittingObserver {
    fn on_restart_decision(&self, _child: &str, _decision: RestartDecision) {
        // Could emit a new event variant if needed
    }
    
    fn on_backoff_start(&self, _child: &str, _delay: Duration) {
        // Backoff info is included in ChildRestarted event
    }
    
    fn on_limit_exceeded(&self, context: LimitContext) {
        match context {
            LimitContext::PerChild { name, count } => {
                let _ = self.tx.send(SupervisorEvent::ChildRestartLimitExceeded {
                    name,
                    restarts: count,
                });
            }
            LimitContext::Global { count } => {
                let _ = self.tx.send(SupervisorEvent::RestartIntensityExceeded {
                    total_restarts: count,
                });
            }
        }
    }
}
```

### 2. Usage Example: How Supervisor Calls It

```rust
impl SupervisorRunner {
    async fn handle_child_exit(&mut self, task_id: TaskId, exit: ChildExit) -> Result<()> {
        let Some(name) = self.task_map.remove(&task_id) else {
            return Ok(());
        };
        
        let old_gen = self.children.get(&name).map(|c| c.generation).unwrap_or(0);
        let hung = self.children.get(&name).map(|c| c.hung).unwrap_or(false);
        
        // Mark child as dead
        if let Some(child) = self.children.get_mut(&name) {
            child.alive = false;
            child.child_cancel = None;
            child.progress = None;
            child.hung = false;
        }
        
        self.emit(SupervisorEvent::ChildExited {
            name: name.clone(),
            generation: old_gen,
            exit,
        });
        
        if self.cancel.is_cancelled() {
            return Ok(());
        }
        
        // === NEW: Delegate to RestartManager ===
        let child_metadata: HashMap<String, ChildMetadata> = self
            .children
            .iter()
            .map(|(n, c)| {
                (
                    n.clone(),
                    ChildMetadata {
                        alive: c.alive,
                        generation: c.generation,
                        restart_policy: c.spec.restart_policy.clone(),
                    },
                )
            })
            .collect();
        
        let plan = self.restart_manager.evaluate_exit(
            &name,
            &exit,
            hung,
            &self.child_order,
            &child_metadata,
        );
        
        // Handle global limit exceeded
        if let Some(LimitContext::Global { count }) = plan.limit_exceeded {
            self.drain_all().await;
            return Err(SupervisorError::RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts: count });
        }
        
        // Execute restart plan: spawn futures for each target
        for (target_name, delay) in plan.targets {
            let restart_mgr = self.restart_manager.clone(); // Arc<Mutex<RestartManager>>
            let children = self.children.clone(); // Or pass necessary state
            
            // Spawn backoff future (does NOT block supervisor loop!)
            tokio::spawn(async move {
                tokio::time::sleep(delay).await;
                
                // Send command back to supervisor to perform actual restart
                // (Supervisor loop handles the respawn via command channel)
                let _ = command_tx.send(SupervisorCommand::RestartChild {
                    name: target_name,
                    old_gen,
                }).await;
            });
        }
        
        Ok(())
    }
}
```

**Key insight:** The manager returns a **plan** with target names and delays. The supervisor spawns independent `tokio::spawn` futures for each backoff delay, which send restart commands back through the supervisor's command channel. This keeps the supervisor loop non-blocking.

### 3. Complexity Hidden Internally

The RestartManager hides:

1. **Policy evaluation logic** (Permanent/Transient/Temporary semantics)
2. **Backoff calculation** (exponential growth, cap enforcement)
3. **Limit tracking** (sliding window timestamp management, eviction)
4. **Strategy coordination** (OneForOne vs OneForAll target selection)
5. **Event emission** (via pluggable observer)
6. **History management** (timestamp lists, generation counters)
7. **Order preservation** (for OneForAll cascades)
8. **Hung-child handling** (treating hung exits as failures regardless of ChildExit variant)

The supervisor only needs to:
- Call `evaluate_exit()` when a child dies
- Spawn backoff futures for the returned plan
- Execute the actual respawn (factory call, mailbox swap, etc.)

### 4. Dependency Strategy

**What RestartManager needs injected:**

1. `RestartManagerConfig` (strategy, global limiter, observer) — injected at construction
2. Per-child `ChildRestartConfig` (policy, backoff, limiter) — registered via `add_child()`
3. Exit event data (child name, ChildExit, hung flag) — passed to `evaluate_exit()`
4. Supervisor state snapshots (child_order, metadata) — passed to `evaluate_exit()`

**What RestartManager owns:**

1. All restart histories (timestamps, generation counters)
2. Child-specific configurations (policy, backoff, limiter)
3. References to pluggable strategies/policies (via Arc)

**What supervisor owns:**

1. Child factory invocation
2. JoinSet / task spawning
3. Mailbox swapping (hot-reload)
4. Peer map construction
5. Backoff future spawning (to avoid blocking)
6. Event broadcast sender

This clean separation means RestartManager is:
- **Testable in isolation** (no async, no I/O, pure decision logic)
- **Reusable** (could supervise non-agent children)
- **Stateless regarding supervisor internals** (no JoinSet, no mailboxes)

### 5. Trade-offs

**What You Gain:**

1. **Maximum flexibility:**
   - Swap in custom restart policies (e.g., "restart only on specific error codes")
   - Implement exotic backoff algorithms (jittered, Fibonacci, adaptive)
   - Add custom strategies (RestForOne, dependency-aware restarts)
   - Integrate with external metrics/logging via observer
   - Extend without modifying core logic

2. **Non-blocking by design:**
   - `evaluate_exit()` is synchronous — no await points
   - Backoff delays are returned as durations, spawned as futures by supervisor
   - No `tokio::time::sleep()` inside manager

3. **Testability:**
   - All extension points are traits — easy to mock
   - Restart decisions are pure functions of state
   - No hidden global state or side effects

4. **Separation of concerns:**
   - Policy logic (when to restart) separate from strategy (what to restart)
   - Limit enforcement (frequency) separate from backoff (timing)
   - Event emission separate from decision logic

5. **Composability:**
   - Chain multiple observers (metrics + logging + alerts)
   - Combine strategies (OneForOne with dependency overrides)
   - Reuse backoff/limiter implementations across projects

6. **Future-proof:**
   - Add new policy types without breaking existing code
   - Introduce new event types via observer
   - Support dynamic configuration updates (swap Arc'd traits)

**What You Lose:**

1. **Complexity for simple cases:**
   - Users who just want "restart 3 times in 60 seconds" face trait soup
   - Mitigation: Provide `RestartManagerBuilder` with sane defaults

2. **Indirection overhead:**
   - Trait dispatch adds virtual call overhead (minimal in practice)
   - Arc cloning for shared policies (cheap, but not free)

3. **Type erasure challenges:**
   - Can't downcast `dyn RestartPolicy` to check if it's `Temporary`
   - Mitigation: Add `policy_type()` method or separate flags in metadata

4. **Configuration burden:**
   - Users must wire up traits even if they want standard behavior
   - Mitigation: Provide `StandardRestartManager::new()` with built-ins

5. **No compile-time checks on strategy correctness:**
   - A buggy `SupervisorStrategy` could return invalid names
   - Mitigation: Document contracts clearly, add debug assertions

6. **Learning curve:**
   - New contributors must understand 5+ traits before modifying restart logic
   - Mitigation: Excellent docs + examples for common cases

**Overall assessment:** This design prioritizes **flexibility and extensibility** over simplicity. It's ideal for a framework where users have diverse restart requirements (ML training, distributed systems, long-running services). If the goal is "just restart agents that crash," this is overengineered. But given the constraint to "MAXIMIZE FLEXIBILITY," this trait-based approach hits the target.

---

## Extension Examples

To demonstrate flexibility, here are some extension scenarios:

### Custom Backoff: Jittered Exponential

```rust
pub struct JitteredExponentialBackoff {
    base: Duration,
    max: Duration,
    jitter_pct: f64,
}

impl BackoffStrategy for JitteredExponentialBackoff {
    fn compute_delay(&self, history: &RestartHistory) -> Duration {
        let n = history.timestamps.len().saturating_sub(1) as u32;
        let base_delay = self.base.saturating_mul(2u32.pow(n)).min(self.max);
        
        let jitter_range = base_delay.as_secs_f64() * self.jitter_pct;
        let jitter = rand::random::<f64>() * jitter_range;
        base_delay + Duration::from_secs_f64(jitter)
    }
}
```

### Custom Strategy: RestForOne (Erlang-style)

```rust
pub struct RestForOneStrategy;

impl SupervisorStrategy for RestForOneStrategy {
    fn select_targets<'a>(
        &self,
        crashed: &str,
        all_children: &'a [String],
        _states: &HashMap<String, &ChildMetadata>,
    ) -> Vec<&'a str> {
        // Restart crashed child + all children started after it
        let mut found_crashed = false;
        all_children
            .iter()
            .filter(|name| {
                if name.as_str() == crashed {
                    found_crashed = true;
                }
                found_crashed
            })
            .map(|s| s.as_str())
            .collect()
    }
}
```

### Custom Observer: Prometheus Metrics

```rust
pub struct MetricsObserver {
    restart_counter: prometheus::IntCounter,
    backoff_histogram: prometheus::Histogram,
}

impl RestartObserver for MetricsObserver {
    fn on_restart_decision(&self, child: &str, decision: RestartDecision) {
        if matches!(decision, RestartDecision::Restart) {
            self.restart_counter.inc();
        }
    }
    
    fn on_backoff_start(&self, _child: &str, delay: Duration) {
        self.backoff_histogram.observe(delay.as_secs_f64());
    }
    
    fn on_limit_exceeded(&self, _context: LimitContext) {
        // Could emit alert to PagerDuty here
    }
}
```

---

This design provides maximum flexibility through trait-based extension points while maintaining clean separation between decision logic (synchronous) and execution (asynchronous). The supervisor remains simple: ask the manager "what should I do?" and execute the plan.

agentId: ab36433 (for resuming to continue this agent's work if needed)
```
## Agent (2026-03-28 23:42:08)

## Three Interface Designs for RestartManager

---

### Design 1: Minimal Interface (1 entry point)

**Philosophy:** Hide maximum complexity behind minimal API surface.

```rust
pub struct RestartManager { /* internal state */ }

pub enum RestartDecision {
    Restart { delay: Duration },
    RestartAll,
    Skip,
    ChildLimitExceeded { restarts: u64 },
    IntensityExceeded { total_restarts: u64 },
}

impl RestartManager {
    pub fn new(config: RestartConfig, event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>) -> Self;
    
    /// THE ONLY ENTRY POINT
    pub fn decide(
        &mut self,
        child_name: &str,
        exit: &ChildExit,
        policy: &ChildRestart,
        was_hung: bool,
    ) -> RestartDecision;
}
```

**Usage:**
```rust
let decision = self.restart_mgr.decide(&name, &exit, &policy, was_hung);
match decision {
    RestartDecision::Restart { delay } => {
        tokio::spawn(async move {
            tokio::time::sleep(delay).await;
            restart_tx.send(RestartCommand { name }).await;
        });
    }
    // ...
}
```

**Hides:** Dual tracker coordination, backoff math, event emission, hung override, policy logic.

**Trade-offs:**
| Gain | Lose |
|------|------|
| Single call site, ~100 LOC reduction | Supervisor must spawn delay futures |
| Event emission centralized | Can't consult async oracles (external rate limiter) |
| Testable (mock event_tx, inject time) | OneForAll still needs supervisor coordination |

---

### Design 2: Maximum Flexibility (Trait-based extension)

**Philosophy:** Support custom strategies, pluggable backoff, external observers.

```rust
// Extension points
pub trait RestartPolicy: Send + Sync {
    fn should_restart(&self, exit: &ChildExit, hung: bool) -> bool;
}

pub trait BackoffStrategy: Send + Sync {
    fn compute_delay(&self, history: &RestartHistory) -> Duration;
}

pub trait RestartLimiter: Send + Sync {
    fn record(&mut self, now: Instant);
    fn exceeded(&self) -> bool;
}

pub trait SupervisorStrategy: Send + Sync {
    fn select_targets<'a>(&self, crashed: &str, all: &'a [String]) -> Vec<&'a str>;
}

pub trait RestartObserver: Send + Sync {
    fn on_restart_decision(&self, child: &str, decision: RestartDecision);
    fn on_limit_exceeded(&self, context: LimitContext);
}

// Main interface
pub struct RestartManager { /* trait objects */ }

pub struct RestartPlan {
    pub targets: Vec<(String, Duration)>,
    pub limit_exceeded: Option<LimitContext>,
}

impl RestartManager {
    pub fn new(config: RestartManagerConfig) -> Self;
    pub fn add_child(&mut self, name: String, config: ChildRestartConfig);
    pub fn remove_child(&mut self, name: &str);
    
    pub fn evaluate_exit(
        &mut self,
        child_name: &str,
        exit: &ChildExit,
        hung: bool,
        child_order: &[String],
        metadata: &HashMap<String, ChildMetadata>,
    ) -> RestartPlan;
}
```

**Usage:**
```rust
// Custom jittered backoff
struct JitteredBackoff { base: Duration, max: Duration, jitter: f64 }
impl BackoffStrategy for JitteredBackoff { /* ... */ }

// Prometheus metrics observer
struct MetricsObserver { counter: IntCounter }
impl RestartObserver for MetricsObserver { /* ... */ }

// Wire up
let config = RestartManagerConfig {
    strategy: Arc::new(OneForOneStrategy),
    global_limiter: Box::new(SlidingWindowLimiter::new(10, Duration::from_secs(60))),
    observer: Arc::new(MetricsObserver::new()),
};
let mut mgr = RestartManager::new(config);
```

**Trade-offs:**
| Gain | Lose |
|------|------|
| Custom backoff (jitter, Fibonacci, adaptive) | Complex for simple cases (trait soup) |
| Custom strategies (RestForOne, dependency-aware) | Virtual dispatch overhead (minimal) |
| Composable observers (metrics + logging + alerts) | Learning curve for contributors |
| Future-proof (add policies without breaking) | Configuration burden |

---

### Design 3: Ergonomic Default Case (80% trivial)

**Philosophy:** One-liner for common case, power available when needed.

```rust
pub struct RestartManager { /* internal state */ }

pub enum RestartDecision {
    RestartAfter { delay: Duration },
    RestartAll,
    NoRestart,
    ChildLimitExceeded { restarts: u64 },
    IntensityExceeded { total_restarts: u64 },
}

impl RestartManager {
    pub fn new(config: SupervisorConfig) -> Self;
    pub fn register(&mut self, name: &str, spec: &ChildSpec);
    pub fn unregister(&mut self, name: &str);
    
    /// The one-liner: "This child exited — what should I do?"
    pub fn decide(&mut self, name: &str, exit: &ChildExit, now: Instant) -> RestartDecision;
    
    /// For OneForAll: record restart for all non-Temporary children
    pub fn record_all(&mut self, now: Instant);
    
    /// Get backoff delay for a specific child (useful for cascade ordering)
    pub fn backoff_delay(&self, name: &str) -> Duration;
}
```

**Usage:**
```rust
// Common case: ONE LINE
let decision = self.restart_mgr.decide(&name, &exit, Instant::now());

match decision {
    RestartDecision::RestartAfter { delay } => {
        self.pending_restarts.push(PendingRestart { name, when: Instant::now() + delay });
    }
    RestartDecision::RestartAll => self.cascade_restart_all().await,
    // ...
}
```

**Supervisor loop handles delays non-blockingly:**
```rust
tokio::select! {
    // ... existing branches ...
    
    _ = self.next_restart_ready(), if !self.pending_restarts.is_empty() => {
        let restart = self.pending_restarts.pop().unwrap();
        self.spawn_child(&restart.name).await?;
    }
}
```

**Trade-offs:**
| Gain | Lose |
|------|------|
| 80% case is 1 line | Not extensible (no trait hooks) |
| Explicit `Instant` injection = testable | Must call `register()` on child start |
| Type-safe enum forces handling all cases | OneForAll still needs `record_all()` helper |
| No hidden state, easy to debug | Supervisor wires up pending restart queue |

---

## Comparison

| Aspect | Design 1 (Minimal) | Design 2 (Flexible) | Design 3 (Ergonomic) |
|--------|-------------------|--------------------|--------------------|
| **Entry points** | 1 (`decide`) | 3 (`evaluate_exit`, `add_child`, `remove_child`) | 3 (`decide`, `register`, `unregister`) |
| **Extensibility** | None | Maximum (5 traits) | None |
| **Simple case LOC** | ~10 | ~30 (setup) | ~5 |
| **Event emission** | Inside manager | Via observer trait | Outside (supervisor) |
| **Time injection** | Implicit `Instant::now()` | Explicit `now` param | Explicit `now` param |
| **Backoff blocking** | No (returns delay) | No (returns plan) | No (returns delay) |
| **Testing** | Mock event_tx | Mock all traits | Inject Instant |

---

## My Recommendation

**Design 3 (Ergonomic)** is the strongest fit for this codebase.

**Why:**

1. **Matches the codebase philosophy** — mra values simplicity ("i just want something lightweight and make me happy"). Design 2's trait soup contradicts this.

2. **Solves the actual problems:**
   - Scattered logic → consolidated in `decide()`
   - Blocking backoff → returns `Duration`, supervisor schedules
   - Hard to test → explicit `Instant` injection

3. **Minimal migration cost** — existing `RestartTracker` and `IntensityTracker` can be absorbed with small changes. Design 2 would require rewriting everything as trait impls.

4. **Right level of abstraction** — supervisor still owns spawning/events (its job), but decision logic is cleanly extracted.

5. **Future-compatible** — if you later need Design 2's flexibility, you can evolve Design 3's `decide()` to take a trait object. Starting minimal is easier than starting complex.

**Suggested hybrid improvement:** Add one method from Design 1:

```rust
impl RestartManager {
    pub fn new(config: SupervisorConfig, event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>) -> Self;
}
```

This lets the manager emit events internally (like Design 1) while keeping the ergonomic API. Events are context-free enough to centralize.

---

### Tool Call [completed]: `gh issue create --repo yuann3/mra --title "RFC: Extract RestartManager to consolidate restart logic" --body "$(cat <<'EOF'
## Summary

Extract restart decision logic from \`SupervisorRunner\` into a dedicated \`RestartManager\` struct. This consolidates ~400 lines scattered across 3 files into a single module with a clean interface.

## Problem

Restart logic is currently scattered across:

- \`supervisor/runner.rs\` — \`handle_child_exit()\` (150 lines), \`restart_all()\` (100 lines)
- \`supervisor/tracker.rs\` — \`RestartTracker\` (per-child), \`IntensityTracker\` (global)
- \`supervisor/config.rs\` — \`RestartPolicy\`, \`RestartIntensity\`, \`ChildRestart\` enums

**Pain points:**

1. **Understanding "why didn't my agent restart?" requires 4 file bounces** — runner.rs (hung check) → config.rs (policy) → tracker.rs (per-child limit) → tracker.rs (global intensity)

2. **Two similar but different trackers** — \`RestartTracker\` (exponential backoff + window) vs \`IntensityTracker\` (linear count in window). Both have \`max_restarts\` + \`window\` but different semantics.

3. **\`restart_all()\` duplicates logic from \`handle_child_exit()\`** — similar but subtly different (no per-child backoff in cascade)

4. **Backoff blocks the supervisor loop:**
   \`\`\`rust
   let delay = child.tracker.backoff_delay();
   tokio::time::sleep(delay).await;  // Blocks entire supervisor!
   \`\`\`

5. **No tests for the combined restart path** — individual tracker tests pass, but "hung → cancelled → backoff → intensity check → restart" is untested

## Proposed Solution

New \`RestartManager\` with ergonomic interface optimized for the common case:

\`\`\`rust
pub struct RestartManager {
    strategy: Strategy,
    children: HashMap<String, ChildRestartState>,
    intensity: IntensityTracker,
    event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>,
}

pub enum RestartDecision {
    RestartAfter { delay: Duration },
    RestartAll,
    NoRestart,
    ChildLimitExceeded { restarts: u64 },
    IntensityExceeded { total_restarts: u64 },
}

impl RestartManager {
    pub fn new(
        config: SupervisorConfig,
        event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>,
    ) -> Self;

    pub fn register(&mut self, name: &str, spec: &ChildSpec);
    pub fn unregister(&mut self, name: &str);

    /// The one-liner: "This child exited — what should I do?"
    pub fn decide(
        &mut self,
        name: &str,
        exit: &ChildExit,
        hung: bool,
        now: Instant,
    ) -> RestartDecision;

    /// For OneForAll: record restart for all non-Temporary children
    pub fn record_all(&mut self, now: Instant);

    /// Get backoff delay for a specific child
    pub fn backoff_delay(&self, name: &str) -> Duration;
}
\`\`\`

### Usage in supervisor

**Before (~100 LOC inline):**
\`\`\`rust
let is_failure = if child.hung { true } else { exit.is_failure() };
let should_restart = child.spec.restart.should_restart(is_failure);
if !should_restart { return Ok(()); }

match self.config.strategy {
    Strategy::OneForOne => {
        child.tracker.record(now);
        if child.tracker.exceeded() { /* emit, return */ }
        self.intensity.record(now);
        if self.intensity.exceeded() { /* drain, error */ }
        let delay = child.tracker.backoff_delay();
        tokio::time::sleep(delay).await;  // BLOCKS!
        // ... spawn logic ...
    }
    Strategy::OneForAll => { /* 50 more lines */ }
}
\`\`\`

**After (~15 LOC):**
\`\`\`rust
let decision = self.restart_mgr.decide(&name, &exit, was_hung, Instant::now());

match decision {
    RestartDecision::RestartAfter { delay } => {
        // Non-blocking: schedule for later
        self.pending_restarts.push(PendingRestart { name, when: Instant::now() + delay });
    }
    RestartDecision::RestartAll => {
        self.cascade_restart_all().await
    }
    RestartDecision::NoRestart => {}
    RestartDecision::ChildLimitExceeded { .. } => {}
    RestartDecision::IntensityExceeded { total_restarts } => {
        self.drain_all().await;
        return Err(SupervisorError::RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts });
    }
}
\`\`\`

**New select branch for non-blocking delays:**
\`\`\`rust
tokio::select! {
    // ... existing branches ...

    _ = self.next_restart_ready(), if !self.pending_restarts.is_empty() => {
        let restart = self.pending_restarts.pop().unwrap();
        self.do_start_child(&restart.name).await?;
    }
}
\`\`\`

## What RestartManager Hides

1. **Dual tracker coordination** — per-child vs global, checked in correct order
2. **Policy evaluation** — Permanent/Transient/Temporary + hung override
3. **Exponential backoff math** — \`2^n * base\`, capped at max
4. **Sliding window eviction** — old timestamps pruned on \`record()\`
5. **Event emission** — \`ChildRestartLimitExceeded\`, \`IntensityExceeded\`
6. **Strategy dispatch** — OneForOne returns delay, OneForAll signals cascade

## What Supervisor Still Owns

- Child spawning (factory, JoinSet, mailbox swap)
- Peer map construction
- Delay scheduling (via \`pending_restarts\` queue)
- Cancellation handling
- OneForAll cascade ordering (knows child insertion order)

## Design Decisions

### Why not trait-based extensibility?

Considered a design with pluggable \`BackoffStrategy\`, \`RestartPolicy\`, \`SupervisorStrategy\` traits. Rejected because:

- Contradicts codebase philosophy ("lightweight and make me happy")
- Adds complexity for hypothetical future needs
- Can evolve to traits later if needed

### Why explicit \`Instant\` parameter?

\`\`\`rust
pub fn decide(&mut self, ..., now: Instant) -> RestartDecision
\`\`\`

Makes testing trivial — inject fake timestamps without mocking \`Instant::now()\`.

### Why return \`Duration\` instead of sleeping?

Returning the delay instead of \`await\`ing it:
- Keeps supervisor loop responsive
- Allows cancellation during backoff (check generation before restart)
- Enables batching/prioritization of pending restarts

## Implementation Plan

1. Create \`supervisor/restart_manager.rs\` with \`RestartManager\` struct
2. Move \`RestartTracker\` and \`IntensityTracker\` into restart_manager (or keep in tracker.rs and import)
3. Add \`register()\`/\`unregister()\` calls in \`do_start_child()\`/child removal
4. Replace inline restart logic in \`handle_child_exit()\` with \`decide()\` call
5. Add \`pending_restarts: Vec<PendingRestart>\` to \`SupervisorRunner\`
6. Add new \`select!\` branch for delayed restarts
7. Update \`restart_all()\` to use \`record_all()\` + cascade logic
8. Add tests for combined restart paths (the current gap)

## Test Plan

- [ ] Unit tests for \`RestartManager::decide()\` covering all \`RestartDecision\` variants
- [ ] Test per-child limit exceeded path
- [ ] Test global intensity exceeded path
- [ ] Test OneForAll triggers \`RestartAll\` decision
- [ ] Test hung child forces failure even on \`ChildExit::Shutdown\`
- [ ] Test backoff delay increases exponentially
- [ ] Integration test: "hung → cancelled → backoff → restart" full path
- [ ] Integration test: delayed restart respects cancellation

## Migration

Non-breaking. \`RestartManager\` is internal to supervisor module. External API unchanged.
EOF

## Summary

Extract restart decision logic from `SupervisorRunner` into a dedicated `RestartManager` struct. This consolidates ~400 lines scattered across 3 files into a single module with a clean interface.

## Problem

Restart logic is currently scattered across:

- `supervisor/runner.rs` — `handle_child_exit()` (150 lines), `restart_all()` (100 lines)
- `supervisor/tracker.rs` — `RestartTracker` (per-child), `IntensityTracker` (global)
- `supervisor/config.rs` — `RestartPolicy`, `RestartIntensity`, `ChildRestart` enums

**Pain points:**

1. **Understanding "why didn't my agent restart?" requires 4 file bounces** — runner.rs (hung check) → config.rs (policy) → tracker.rs (per-child limit) → tracker.rs (global intensity)

2. **Two similar but different trackers** — `RestartTracker` (exponential backoff + window) vs `IntensityTracker` (linear count in window). Both have `max_restarts` + `window` but different semantics.

3. **`restart_all()` duplicates logic from `handle_child_exit()`** — similar but subtly different (no per-child backoff in cascade)

4. **Backoff blocks the supervisor loop:**
   ```rust
   let delay = child.tracker.backoff_delay();
   tokio::time::sleep(delay).await;  // Blocks entire supervisor!
   ```

5. **No tests for the combined restart path** — individual tracker tests pass, but "hung → cancelled → backoff → intensity check → restart" is untested

## Proposed Solution

New `RestartManager` with ergonomic interface optimized for the common case:

```rust
pub struct RestartManager {
    strategy: Strategy,
    children: HashMap<String, ChildRestartState>,
    intensity: IntensityTracker,
    event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>,
}

pub enum RestartDecision {
    RestartAfter { delay: Duration },
    RestartAll,
    NoRestart,
    ChildLimitExceeded { restarts: u64 },
    IntensityExceeded { total_restarts: u64 },
}

impl RestartManager {
    pub fn new(
        config: SupervisorConfig,
        event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>,
    ) -> Self;

    pub fn register(&mut self, name: &str, spec: &ChildSpec);
    pub fn unregister(&mut self, name: &str);

    /// The one-liner: "This child exited — what should I do?"
    pub fn decide(
        &mut self,
        name: &str,
        exit: &ChildExit,
        hung: bool,
        now: Instant,
    ) -> RestartDecision;

    /// For OneForAll: record restart for all non-Temporary children
    pub fn record_all(&mut self, now: Instant);

    /// Get backoff delay for a specific child
    pub fn backoff_delay(&self, name: &str) -> Duration;
}
```

### Usage in supervisor

**Before (~100 LOC inline):**
```rust
let is_failure = if child.hung { true } else { exit.is_failure() };
let should_restart = child.spec.restart.should_restart(is_failure);
if !should_restart { return Ok(()); }

match self.config.strategy {
    Strategy::OneForOne => {
        child.tracker.record(now);
        if child.tracker.exceeded() { /* emit, return */ }
        self.intensity.record(now);
        if self.intensity.exceeded() { /* drain, error */ }
        let delay = child.tracker.backoff_delay();
        tokio::time::sleep(delay).await;  // BLOCKS!
        // ... spawn logic ...
    }
    Strategy::OneForAll => { /* 50 more lines */ }
}
```

**After (~15 LOC):**
```rust
let decision = self.restart_mgr.decide(&name, &exit, was_hung, Instant::now());

match decision {
    RestartDecision::RestartAfter { delay } => {
        // Non-blocking: schedule for later
        self.pending_restarts.push(PendingRestart { name, when: Instant::now() + delay });
    }
    RestartDecision::RestartAll => {
        self.cascade_restart_all().await
    }
    RestartDecision::NoRestart => {}
    RestartDecision::ChildLimitExceeded { .. } => {}
    RestartDecision::IntensityExceeded { total_restarts } => {
        self.drain_all().await;
        return Err(SupervisorError::RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts });
    }
}
```

**New select branch for non-blocking delays:**
```rust
tokio::select! {
    // ... existing branches ...

    _ = self.next_restart_ready(), if !self.pending_restarts.is_empty() => {
        let restart = self.pending_restarts.pop().unwrap();
        self.do_start_child(&restart.name).await?;
    }
}
```

## What RestartManager Hides

1. **Dual tracker coordination** — per-child vs global, checked in correct order
2. **Policy evaluation** — Permanent/Transient/Temporary + hung override
3. **Exponential backoff math** — `2^n * base`, capped at max
4. **Sliding window eviction** — old timestamps pruned on `record()`
5. **Event emission** — `ChildRestartLimitExceeded`, `IntensityExceeded`
6. **Strategy dispatch** — OneForOne returns delay, OneForAll signals cascade

## What Supervisor Still Owns

- Child spawning (factory, JoinSet, mailbox swap)
- Peer map construction
- Delay scheduling (via `pending_restarts` queue)
- Cancellation handling
- OneForAll cascade ordering (knows child insertion order)

## Design Decisions

### Why not trait-based extensibility?

Considered a design with pluggable `BackoffStrategy`, `RestartPolicy`, `SupervisorStrategy` traits. Rejected because:

- Contradicts codebase philosophy ("lightweight and make me happy")
- Adds complexity for hypothetical future needs
- Can evolve to traits later if needed

### Why explicit `Instant` parameter?

```rust
pub fn decide(&mut self, ..., now: Instant) -> RestartDecision
```

Makes testing trivial — inject fake timestamps without mocking `Instant::now()`.

### Why return `Duration` instead of sleeping?

Returning the delay instead of `await`ing it:
- Keeps supervisor loop responsive
- Allows cancellation during backoff (check generation before restart)
- Enables batching/prioritization of pending restarts

## Implementation Plan

1. Create `supervisor/restart_manager.rs` with `RestartManager` struct
2. Move `RestartTracker` and `IntensityTracker` into restart_manager (or keep in tracker.rs and import)
3. Add `register()`/`unregister()` calls in `do_start_child()`/child removal
4. Replace inline restart logic in `handle_child_exit()` with `decide()` call
5. Add `pending_restarts: Vec<PendingRestart>` to `SupervisorRunner`
6. Add new `select!` branch for delayed restarts
7. Update `restart_all()` to use `record_all()` + cascade logic
8. Add tests for combined restart paths (the current gap)

## Test Plan

- [ ] Unit tests for `RestartManager::decide()` covering all `RestartDecision` variants
- [ ] Test per-child limit exceeded path
- [ ] Test global intensity exceeded path
- [ ] Test OneForAll triggers `RestartAll` decision
- [ ] Test hung child forces failure even on `ChildExit::Shutdown`
- [ ] Test backoff delay increases exponentially
- [ ] Integration test: "hung → cancelled → backoff → restart" full path
- [ ] Integration test: delayed restart respects cancellation

## Migration

Non-breaking. `RestartManager` is internal to supervisor module. External API unchanged.
EOF
)"

https://github.com/yuann3/mra/issues/8
```

```
use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::sync::Arc;
use std::time::Duration;

use tokio::sync::{broadcast, mpsc, watch};
use tokio::task::JoinSet;
use tokio_util::sync::CancellationToken;

use crate::agent::AgentHandle;
use crate::agent::ProgressState;
use crate::agent::mailbox::MailboxSlot;
use crate::budget::BudgetTracker;
use crate::error::SupervisorError;
use crate::ids::AgentId;
use crate::tool::ToolRegistry;

use super::ChildExit;
use super::child::{ChildContext, ChildSpec};
use super::config::{ChildRestart, Strategy, SupervisorConfig};
use super::event::SupervisorEvent;
use super::handle::SupervisorCommand;
use super::tracker::{IntensityTracker, RestartTracker};

struct ChildState {
    spec: ChildSpec,
    id: AgentId,
    generation: u64,
    progress: Option<watch::Receiver<ProgressState>>,
    child_cancel: Option<CancellationToken>,
    mailbox: Arc<MailboxSlot>,
    logical_cancel: CancellationToken,
    tracker: RestartTracker,
    alive: bool,
    hung: bool,
}

pub(crate) struct SupervisorRunner {
    config: SupervisorConfig,
    children: HashMap<String, ChildState>,
    child_order: Vec<String>,
    task_map: HashMap<tokio::task::Id, String>,
    join_set: JoinSet<ChildExit>,
    command_rx: mpsc::Receiver<SupervisorCommand>,
    event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>,
    cancel: CancellationToken,
    intensity: IntensityTracker,
    budget: Option<Arc<BudgetTracker>>,
}

impl SupervisorRunner {
    pub(crate) fn new(
        config: SupervisorConfig,
        command_rx: mpsc::Receiver<SupervisorCommand>,
        event_tx: broadcast::Sender<SupervisorEvent>,
        budget: Option<Arc<BudgetTracker>>,
    ) -> Self {
        let intensity = IntensityTracker::new(config.intensity.clone());
        Self {
            config,
            children: HashMap::new(),
            child_order: Vec::new(),
            task_map: HashMap::new(),
            join_set: JoinSet::new(),
            command_rx,
            event_tx,
            cancel: CancellationToken::new(),
            intensity,
            budget,
        }
    }

    pub(crate) async fn run(mut self) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        let mut hang_tick = tokio::time::interval(self.config.hang_check_interval);
        hang_tick.set_missed_tick_behavior(tokio::time::MissedTickBehavior::Skip);

        self.emit(SupervisorEvent::SupervisorStarted);

        loop {
            tokio::select! {
                _ = self.cancel.cancelled() => {
                    self.drain_all().await;
                    break Ok(());
                }

                Some(result) = self.join_set.join_next_with_id() => {
                    self.handle_child_exit(result).await?;
                }

                cmd = self.command_rx.recv() => match cmd {
                    None => {
                        self.drain_all().await;
                        break Ok(());
                    }
                    Some(cmd) => self.handle_command(cmd).await?,
                },

                _ = hang_tick.tick() => {
                    self.check_hangs().await;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    fn emit(&self, event: SupervisorEvent) {
        let _ = self.event_tx.send(event);
    }

    async fn handle_command(&mut self, cmd: SupervisorCommand) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        match cmd {
            SupervisorCommand::StartChild { spec, reply } => {
                let result = self.do_start_child(spec).await;
                let _ = reply.send(result);
            }
            SupervisorCommand::StopChild { name, reply } => {
                let result = self.do_stop_child(&name).await;
                let _ = reply.send(result);
            }
            SupervisorCommand::GetChild { name, reply } => {
                let handle = self.children.get(&name).map(|child| {
                    AgentHandle::new(
                        child.id,
                        child.mailbox.clone(),
                        child.logical_cancel.clone(),
                    )
                });
                let _ = reply.send(handle);
            }
            SupervisorCommand::Shutdown => {
                self.drain_all().await;
                self.cancel.cancel();
            }
        }
        Ok(())
    }

    async fn do_start_child(&mut self, spec: ChildSpec) -> Result<AgentHandle, SupervisorError> {
        let name = spec.name.clone();
        let id = AgentId::new();
        let logical_cancel = CancellationToken::new();
        let child_cancel = logical_cancel.child_token();

        // Create stable mailbox with dummy sender
        let (dummy_tx, _) = mpsc::channel(1);
        let mailbox = Arc::new(MailboxSlot::new(dummy_tx));

        // Build peers map from existing alive children
        let peers: HashMap<String, AgentHandle> = self
            .children
            .iter()
            .filter(|(_, c)| c.alive)
            .map(|(n, c)| {
                (
                    n.clone(),
                    AgentHandle::new(c.id, c.mailbox.clone(), c.logical_cancel.clone()),
                )
            })
            .collect();

        // Register agent budget slot if budget tracking is active
        if let Some(ref budget) = self.budget {
            budget.register_agent(&name, spec.token_budget);
        }

        // Call factory
        let ctx = ChildContext {
            id,
            generation: 0,
            cancel: child_cancel.clone(),
            peers,
            llm: None,
            budget: self.budget.clone(),
            tools: ToolRegistry::new(),
        };
        let spawned = (spec.factory)(ctx)
            .await
            .map_err(|e| SupervisorError::SpawnFailed(e.to_string()))?;

        // Swap real sender into stable mailbox
        mailbox.swap(spawned.sender);

        // Build the stable handle
        let handle = AgentHandle::new(id, mailbox.clone(), logical_cancel.clone());

        // Spawn future in JoinSet
        let abort = self.join_set.spawn(spawned.future);
        let task_id = abort.id();
        self.task_map.insert(task_id, name.clone());

        let tracker = RestartTracker::new(&spec.config.restart_policy);

        let state = ChildState {
            spec,
            id,
            generation: 0,
            progress: Some(spawned.progress),
            child_cancel: Some(child_cancel),
            mailbox,
            logical_cancel,
            tracker,
            alive: true,
            hung: false,
        };

        self.children.insert(name.clone(), state);
        self.child_order.push(name.clone());

        self.emit(SupervisorEvent::ChildStarted {
            name,
            generation: 0,
        });

        Ok(handle)
    }

    async fn do_stop_child(&mut self, name: &str) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        let child = self
            .children
            .get_mut(name)
            .ok_or_else(|| SupervisorError::ChildNotFound(name.into()))?;

        if let Some(cancel) = child.child_cancel.take() {
            cancel.cancel();
        }
        child.alive = false;
        Ok(())
    }

    async fn handle_child_exit(
        &mut self,
        result: Result<(tokio::task::Id, ChildExit), tokio::task::JoinError>,
    ) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        let (task_id, exit) = match result {
            Ok((id, exit)) => (id, exit),
            Err(e) => {
                let id = e.id();
                (id, ChildExit::Failed(format!("task panicked: {e}")))
            }
        };

        let Some(name) = self.task_map.remove(&task_id) else {
            return Ok(());
        };

        let (old_gen, should_restart) = {
            let Some(child) = self.children.get_mut(&name) else {
                return Ok(());
            };

            let old_gen = child.generation;
            child.alive = false;
            child.child_cancel = None;
            child.progress = None;

            // Hung children exit with Shutdown, which isn't a "failure" —
            // override so Transient restart policy still kicks in.
            let is_failure = if child.hung {
                child.hung = false;
                true
            } else {
                exit.is_failure()
            };
            let should_restart = child.spec.restart.should_restart(is_failure);
            (old_gen, should_restart)
        };

        let _ = self.event_tx.send(SupervisorEvent::ChildExited {
            name: name.clone(),
            generation: old_gen,
            exit,
        });

        if !should_restart || self.cancel.is_cancelled() {
            return Ok(());
        }

        match self.config.strategy {
            Strategy::OneForOne => {
                // Record in per-child tracker
                let now = tokio::time::Instant::now();
                let child = self.children.get_mut(&name).unwrap();
                child.tracker.record(now);

                if child.tracker.exceeded() {
                    let restarts = child.tracker.total_restarts;
                    let _ = self
                        .event_tx
                        .send(SupervisorEvent::ChildRestartLimitExceeded { name, restarts });
                    return Ok(());
                }

                // Record in per-supervisor intensity tracker
                self.intensity.record(now);
                if self.intensity.exceeded() {
                    let total_restarts = self.intensity.total_restarts;
                    let _ = self
                        .event_tx
                        .send(SupervisorEvent::RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts });
                    self.drain_all().await;
                    return Err(SupervisorError::RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts });
                }

                // Compute backoff delay and sleep
                let child = self.children.get(&name).unwrap();
                let delay = child.tracker.backoff_delay();
                tokio::time::sleep(delay).await;

                // Don't restart if cancelled during backoff sleep
                if self.cancel.is_cancelled() {
                    return Ok(());
                }

                // Build peers map from alive siblings
                let peers: HashMap<String, AgentHandle> = self
                    .children
                    .iter()
                    .filter(|(n, c)| c.alive && *n != &name)
                    .map(|(n, c)| {
                        (
                            n.clone(),
                            AgentHandle::new(c.id, c.mailbox.clone(), c.logical_cancel.clone()),
                        )
                    })
                    .collect();

                let child = self.children.get_mut(&name).unwrap();

                // Increment generation and create new per-generation cancel token
                let new_gen = old_gen + 1;
                let child_cancel = child.logical_cancel.child_token();

                let ctx = ChildContext {
                    id: child.id,
                    generation: new_gen,
                    cancel: child_cancel.clone(),
                    peers,
                    llm: None,
                    budget: self.budget.clone(),
                    tools: ToolRegistry::new(),
                };

                let spawned = match (child.spec.factory)(ctx).await {
                    Ok(s) => s,
                    Err(_) => {
                        // Factory failed — leave child dead
                        return Ok(());
                    }
                };

                // Hot-swap sender into stable mailbox
                child.mailbox.swap(spawned.sender);

                // Spawn new future in JoinSet
                let abort = self.join_set.spawn(spawned.future);
                let new_task_id = abort.id();
                self.task_map.insert(new_task_id, name.clone());

                // Update child state
                child.generation = new_gen;
                child.progress = Some(spawned.progress);
                child.child_cancel = Some(child_cancel);
                child.alive = true;

                let _ = self.event_tx.send(SupervisorEvent::ChildRestarted {
                    name,
                    old_gen,
                    new_gen,
                    delay,
                });
            }
            Strategy::OneForAll => {
                self.restart_all(&name).await?;
            }
        }

        Ok(())
    }

    async fn restart_all(&mut self, trigger_name: &str) -> Result<(), SupervisorError> {
        // 1. Cancel all alive children (except the one that already exited)
        for (name, child) in &self.children {
            if name != trigger_name
                && let Some(ref cancel) = child.child_cancel
            {
                cancel.cancel();
            }
        }

        // 2. Wait for all to exit
        while self.join_set.join_next().await.is_some() {}
        self.task_map.clear();

        // 3. Record restart in per-supervisor intensity tracker
        let now = tokio::time::Instant::now();
        self.intensity.record(now);
        if self.intensity.exceeded() {
            let total = self.intensity.total_restarts;
            let _ = self
                .event_tx
                .send(SupervisorEvent::RestartIntensityExceeded {
                    total_restarts: total,
                });
            self.drain_all().await;
            return Err(SupervisorError::RestartIntensityExceeded {
                total_restarts: total,
            });
        }

        // 4. Respawn all non-Temporary children in insertion order
        let order = self.child_order.clone();
        for child_name in &order {
            // Skip Temporary children
            {
                let child = self.children.get_mut(child_name).unwrap();
                if matches!(child.spec.restart, ChildRestart::Temporary) {
                    child.alive = false;
                    continue;
                }
            }

            if self.cancel.is_cancelled() {
                return Ok(());
            }

            let (old_gen, new_gen, child_cancel, child_id) = {
                let child = self.children.get(child_name).unwrap();
                let old_gen = child.generation;
                let new_gen = old_gen + 1;
                let child_cancel = child.logical_cancel.child_token();
                (old_gen, new_gen, child_cancel, child.id)
            };

            // Build peers from already-respawned siblings
            let peers: HashMap<String, AgentHandle> = self
                .children
                .iter()
                .filter(|(n, c)| c.alive && *n != child_name)
                .map(|(n, c)| {
                    (
                        n.clone(),
                        AgentHandle::new(c.id, c.mailbox.clone(), c.logical_cancel.clone()),
                    )
                })
                .collect();

            let child = self.children.get_mut(child_name).unwrap();
            let ctx = ChildContext {
                id: child_id,
                generation: new_gen,
                cancel: child_cancel.clone(),
                peers,
                llm: None,
                budget: self.budget.clone(),
                tools: ToolRegistry::new(),
            };

            let spawned = match (child.spec.factory)(ctx).await {
                Ok(s) => s,
                Err(_) => {
                    child.alive = false;
                    continue;
                }
            };

            child.mailbox.swap(spawned.sender);
            let abort = self.join_set.spawn(spawned.future);
            self.task_map.insert(abort.id(), child_name.clone());

            child.generation = new_gen;
            child.progress = Some(spawned.progress);
            child.child_cancel = Some(child_cancel);
            child.alive = true;
            child.tracker.record(now);

            let _ = self.event_tx.send(SupervisorEvent::ChildRestarted {
                name: child_name.clone(),
                old_gen,
                new_gen,
                delay: Duration::from_millis(0),
            });
        }

        Ok(())
    }

    async fn drain_all(&mut self) {
        self.emit(SupervisorEvent::SupervisorStopping);
        for child in self.children.values() {
            if let Some(ref cancel) = child.child_cancel {
                cancel.cancel();
            }
        }
        while self.join_set.join_next().await.is_some() {}
    }

    async fn check_hangs(&mut self) {
        let mut hangs = Vec::new();

        for (name, child) in &self.children {
            if !child.alive {
                continue;
            }
            let Some(hang_timeout) = child.spec.hang_timeout else {
                continue;
            };
            let Some(ref progress_rx) = child.progress else {
                continue;
            };

            let progress = progress_rx.borrow();
            if progress.busy && progress.last_progress.elapsed() > hang_timeout {
                let elapsed = progress.last_progress.elapsed();
                hangs.push((name.clone(), child.generation, elapsed));
            }
        }

        for (name, generation, elapsed) in hangs {
            let _ = self.event_tx.send(SupervisorEvent::HangDetected {
                name: name.clone(),
                generation,
                elapsed,
            });

            if let Some(child) = self.children.get_mut(&name)
                && let Some(cancel) = child.child_cancel.take()
            {
                child.hung = true;
                cancel.cancel();
            }
        }
    }
}
```


### Tool Call [completed]: Read /Users/yuan/Developer/mra/src/supervisor/tracker.rs

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-03-28 23:51:06

```
use std::collections::VecDeque;
use std::time::Duration;

use tokio::time::Instant;

use super::config::RestartIntensity;
use crate::config::RestartPolicy;

pub(crate) struct RestartTracker {
    timestamps: VecDeque<Instant>,
    max_restarts: u32,
    window: Duration,
    backoff_base: Duration,
    backoff_max: Duration,
    pub(crate) total_restarts: u64,
}

impl RestartTracker {
    pub(crate) fn new(policy: &RestartPolicy) -> Self {
        Self {
            timestamps: VecDeque::new(),
            max_restarts: policy.max_restarts,
            window: policy.window,
            backoff_base: policy.backoff_base,
            backoff_max: policy.backoff_max,
            total_restarts: 0,
        }
    }

    pub(crate) fn record(&mut self, now: Instant) {
        self.total_restarts += 1;
        self.timestamps.push_back(now);
        let cutoff = now - self.window;
        while self.timestamps.front().is_some_and(|&t| t < cutoff) {
            self.timestamps.pop_front();
        }
    }

    pub(crate) fn exceeded(&self) -> bool {
        self.timestamps.len() > self.max_restarts as usize
    }

    pub(crate) fn backoff_delay(&self) -> Duration {
        let n = self.timestamps.len().saturating_sub(1) as u32;
        let delay = self.backoff_base.saturating_mul(2u32.pow(n));
        delay.min(self.backoff_max)
    }
}

pub(crate) struct IntensityTracker {
    timestamps: VecDeque<Instant>,
    intensity: RestartIntensity,
    pub(crate) total_restarts: u64,
}

impl IntensityTracker {
    pub(crate) fn new(intensity: RestartIntensity) -> Self {
        Self {
            timestamps: VecDeque::new(),
            intensity,
            total_restarts: 0,
        }
    }

    pub(crate) fn record(&mut self, now: Instant) {
        self.total_restarts += 1;
        self.timestamps.push_back(now);
        let cutoff = now - self.intensity.window;
        while self.timestamps.front().is_some_and(|&t| t < cutoff) {
            self.timestamps.pop_front();
        }
    }

    pub(crate) fn exceeded(&self) -> bool {
        self.timestamps.len() > self.intensity.max_restarts as usize
    }
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;
    use crate::config::RestartPolicy;
    use std::time::Duration;
    use tokio::time::Instant;

    fn default_policy() -> RestartPolicy {
        RestartPolicy {
            max_restarts: 3,
            window: Duration::from_secs(60),
            backoff_base: Duration::from_secs(1),
            backoff_max: Duration::from_secs(16),
        }
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn tracker_not_exceeded_within_limit() {
        let mut tracker = RestartTracker::new(&default_policy());
        let now = Instant::now();
        for i in 0..3 {
            tracker.record(now + Duration::from_secs(i));
        }
        assert!(!tracker.exceeded());
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn tracker_exceeded_over_limit() {
        let mut tracker = RestartTracker::new(&default_policy());
        let now = Instant::now();
        for i in 0..4 {
            tracker.record(now + Duration::from_secs(i));
        }
        assert!(tracker.exceeded());
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn tracker_evicts_old_timestamps_outside_window() {
        let policy = RestartPolicy {
            max_restarts: 3,
            window: Duration::from_secs(10),
            backoff_base: Duration::from_secs(1),
            backoff_max: Duration::from_secs(16),
        };
        let mut tracker = RestartTracker::new(&policy);
        let now = Instant::now();
        // Record 3 restarts at t=0,1,2
        for i in 0..3 {
            tracker.record(now + Duration::from_secs(i));
        }
        // Record 1 more at t=15 (outside 10s window, old ones evicted)
        tracker.record(now + Duration::from_secs(15));
        assert!(!tracker.exceeded());
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn tracker_backoff_exponential() {
        let mut tracker = RestartTracker::new(&default_policy());
        let now = Instant::now();

        // 0 timestamps → backoff_base * 2^0 = 1s (but len-1 = 0 when empty... let's record)
        tracker.record(now);
        // len=1, n=0 → 1 * 2^0 = 1s
        assert_eq!(tracker.backoff_delay(), Duration::from_secs(1));

        tracker.record(now + Duration::from_secs(1));
        // len=2, n=1 → 1 * 2^1 = 2s
        assert_eq!(tracker.backoff_delay(), Duration::from_secs(2));

        tracker.record(now + Duration::from_secs(2));
        // len=3, n=2 → 1 * 2^2 = 4s
        assert_eq!(tracker.backoff_delay(), Duration::from_secs(4));
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn tracker_backoff_capped_at_max() {
        let policy = RestartPolicy {
            max_restarts: 10,
            window: Duration::from_secs(60),
            backoff_base: Duration::from_secs(1),
            backoff_max: Duration::from_secs(16),
        };
        let mut tracker = RestartTracker::new(&policy);
        let now = Instant::now();
        // Record enough to make 2^n exceed 16
        for i in 0..6 {
            tracker.record(now + Duration::from_secs(i));
        }
        // len=6, n=5 → 1 * 2^5 = 32, capped to 16
        assert_eq!(tracker.backoff_delay(), Duration::from_secs(16));
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn tracker_total_restarts_counts_all() {
        let policy = RestartPolicy {
            max_restarts: 3,
            window: Duration::from_secs(10),
            backoff_base: Duration::from_secs(1),
            backoff_max: Duration::from_secs(16),
        };
        let mut tracker = RestartTracker::new(&policy);
        let now = Instant::now();
        // Record 3 early, then 2 late (early ones evicted from window)
        for i in 0..3 {
            tracker.record(now + Duration::from_secs(i));
        }
        for i in 0..2 {
            tracker.record(now + Duration::from_secs(20 + i));
        }
        // total_restarts counts all 5, even though window only has 2
        assert_eq!(tracker.total_restarts, 5);
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn intensity_tracker_exceeded() {
        let intensity = RestartIntensity {
            max_restarts: 2,
            window: Duration::from_secs(60),
        };
        let mut tracker = IntensityTracker::new(intensity);
        let now = Instant::now();
        tracker.record(now);
        tracker.record(now + Duration::from_secs(1));
        assert!(!tracker.exceeded());
        tracker.record(now + Duration::from_secs(2));
        assert!(tracker.exceeded());
    }
}
```

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-03-28 23:51:10

```
use std::time::Duration;

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
pub enum Strategy {
    OneForOne,
    OneForAll,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, Default)]
pub enum ChildRestart {
    Permanent,
    #[default]
    Transient,
    Temporary,
}

impl ChildRestart {
    pub fn should_restart(&self, is_failure: bool) -> bool {
        match self {
            Self::Permanent => true,
            Self::Transient => is_failure,
            Self::Temporary => false,
        }
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ShutdownPolicy {
    pub grace: Duration,
}

impl Default for ShutdownPolicy {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            grace: Duration::from_secs(5),
        }
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct RestartIntensity {
    pub max_restarts: u32,
    pub window: Duration,
}

impl Default for RestartIntensity {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            max_restarts: 10,
            window: Duration::from_secs(60),
        }
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct SupervisorConfig {
    pub strategy: Strategy,
    pub intensity: RestartIntensity,
    pub hang_check_interval: Duration,
    pub event_capacity: usize,
}

impl Default for SupervisorConfig {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            strategy: Strategy::OneForOne,
            intensity: RestartIntensity::default(),
            hang_check_interval: Duration::from_secs(1),
            event_capacity: 64,
        }
    }
}
```

```
//! Supervisor system — Erlang/OTP-style agent lifecycle management.

pub(crate) mod child;
mod config;
mod event;
mod handle;
pub(crate) mod runner;
pub(crate) mod tracker;

pub use child::{ChildContext, ChildFactory, ChildSpec, SpawnedChild};
pub use config::{ChildRestart, RestartIntensity, ShutdownPolicy, Strategy, SupervisorConfig};
pub use event::SupervisorEvent;
pub use handle::SupervisorHandle;

/// Why a child agent exited.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub enum ChildExit {
    /// Clean return from the agent's run loop (channel closed, no senders left).
    Normal,
    /// Explicit shutdown via cancellation token or shutdown message.
    Shutdown,
    /// The agent's behavior handler returned an error.
    Failed(String),
}

impl ChildExit {
    /// Returns `true` if this exit should trigger a restart
    /// (for `Transient` or `Permanent` restart policies).
    pub fn is_failure(&self) -> bool {
        matches!(self, Self::Failed(_))
    }
}
```


### Tool Call [completed]: Read /Users/yuan/Developer/mra/src/supervisor/event.rs

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-03-28 23:51:18

```
use std::time::Duration;

use super::ChildExit;

/// Lifecycle events emitted by the supervisor via a `broadcast` channel.
///
/// Subscribe with [`SupervisorHandle::subscribe`](super::SupervisorHandle::subscribe)
/// to observe starts, stops, restarts, and hang detections.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub enum SupervisorEvent {
    /// The supervisor's event loop has started.
    SupervisorStarted,
    /// The supervisor is draining children before shutting down.
    SupervisorStopping,
    /// A child was spawned (or respawned) successfully.
    ChildStarted { name: String, generation: u64 },
    /// A child's run future completed.
    ChildExited {
        name: String,
        generation: u64,
        exit: ChildExit,
    },
    /// A child was restarted after a failure, with the backoff `delay` applied.
    ChildRestarted {
        name: String,
        old_gen: u64,
        new_gen: u64,
        delay: Duration,
    },
    /// A child has been busy without reporting progress longer than its timeout.
    HangDetected {
        name: String,
        generation: u64,
        elapsed: Duration,
    },
    /// A single child hit its per-child restart limit and will not be restarted again.
    ChildRestartLimitExceeded { name: String, restarts: u64 },
    /// Supervisor-wide restart intensity exceeded — the supervisor shuts down.
    RestartIntensityExceeded { total_restarts: u64 },
    /// A token budget was exceeded (reserved for future event-emitter wiring).
    BudgetExceeded { name: String, used: u64, limit: u64 },
}
```
